# Alamofire  Reference

![Alamofire: Elegant Networking in Swift](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Alamofire/Alamofire/master/Resources/AlamofireLogo.png)

[![Swift](https://img.shields.io/badge/Swift-5.9_5.10_6.0-orange?style=flat-square)](https://img.shields.io/badge/Swift-5.9_5.10_6.0-Orange?style=flat-square)
 [![Platforms](https://img.shields.io/badge/Platforms-macOS_iOS_tvOS_watchOS_visionOS_Linux_Windows_Android-yellowgreen?style=flat-square)](https://img.shields.io/badge/Platforms-macOS_iOS_tvOS_watchOS_vision_OS_Linux_Windows_Android-Green?style=flat-square)
 [![CocoaPods Compatible](https://img.shields.io/cocoapods/v/Alamofire.svg?style=flat-square)](https://img.shields.io/cocoapods/v/Alamofire.svg)
 [![Carthage Compatible](https://img.shields.io/badge/Carthage-compatible-4BC51D.svg?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage)
 [![Swift Package Manager](https://img.shields.io/badge/Swift_Package_Manager-compatible-orange?style=flat-square)](https://img.shields.io/badge/Swift_Package_Manager-compatible-orange?style=flat-square)
 [![Swift Forums](https://img.shields.io/badge/Swift_Forums-Alamofire-orange?style=flat-square)](https://forums.swift.org/c/related-projects/alamofire/37)

Alamofire is an HTTP networking library written in Swift.

Features
--------

*   \[x\] Chainable Request / Response Methods
*   \[x\] Swift Concurrency Support Back to iOS 13, macOS 10.15, tvOS 13, and watchOS 6.
*   \[x\] Combine Support
*   \[x\] URL / JSON Parameter Encoding
*   \[x\] Upload File / Data / Stream / MultipartFormData
*   \[x\] Download File using Request or Resume Data
*   \[x\] Authentication with `URLCredential`
*   \[x\] HTTP Response Validation
*   \[x\] Upload and Download Progress Closures with Progress
*   \[x\] cURL Command Output
*   \[x\] Dynamically Adapt and Retry Requests
*   \[x\] TLS Certificate and Public Key Pinning
*   \[x\] Network Reachability
*   \[x\] Comprehensive Unit and Integration Test Coverage
*   \[x\] [Complete Documentation](https://alamofire.github.io/Alamofire)
    

Write Requests Fast!
--------------------

Alamofire’s compact syntax and extensive feature set allow requests with powerful features like automatic retry to be written in just a few lines of code.

    // Automatic String to URL conversion, Swift concurrency support, and automatic retry.
    let response = await AF.request("https://httpbin.org/get", interceptor: .retryPolicy)
                           // Automatic HTTP Basic Auth.
                           .authenticate(username: "user", password: "pass")
                           // Caching customization.
                           .cacheResponse(using: .cache)
                           // Redirect customization.
                           .redirect(using: .follow)
                           // Validate response code and Content-Type.
                           .validate()
                           // Produce a cURL command for the request.
                           .cURLDescription { description in
                             print(description)
                           }
                           // Automatic Decodable support with background parsing.
                           .serializingDecodable(DecodableType.self)
                           // Await the full response with metrics and a parsed body.
                           .response
    // Detailed response description for easy debugging.
    debugPrint(response)
    

Component Libraries
-------------------

In order to keep Alamofire focused specifically on core networking implementations, additional component libraries have been created by the [Alamofire Software Foundation](https://github.com/Alamofire/Foundation)
 to bring additional functionality to the Alamofire ecosystem.

*   [AlamofireImage](https://github.com/Alamofire/AlamofireImage)
     - An image library including image response serializers, `UIImage` and `UIImageView` extensions, custom image filters, an auto-purging in-memory cache, and a priority-based image downloading system.
*   [AlamofireNetworkActivityIndicator](https://github.com/Alamofire/AlamofireNetworkActivityIndicator)
     - Controls the visibility of the network activity indicator on iOS using Alamofire. It contains configurable delay timers to help mitigate flicker and can support `URLSession` instances not managed by Alamofire.

Requirements
------------

| Platform | Minimum Swift Version | Installation | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| iOS 10.0+ / macOS 10.12+ / tvOS 10.0+ / watchOS 3.0+ | 5.9 / Xcode 15.0 | [CocoaPods](#cocoapods)<br>, [Carthage](#carthage)<br>, [Swift Package Manager](#swift-package-manager)<br>, [Manual](#manually) | Fully Tested |
| Linux | Latest Only | [Swift Package Manager](#swift-package-manager) | Building But Unsupported |
| Windows | Latest Only | [Swift Package Manager](#swift-package-manager) | Building But Unsupported |
| Android | Latest Only | [Swift Package Manager](#swift-package-manager) | Building But Unsupported |

#### Known Issues on Linux and Windows

Alamofire builds on Linux, Windows, and Android but there are missing features and many issues in the underlying `swift-corelibs-foundation` that prevent full functionality and may cause crashes. These include:

*   `[ServerTrustManager](Classes/ServerTrustManager.html) ` and associated certificate functionality is unavailable, so there is no certificate pinning and no client certificate support.
*   Various methods of HTTP authentication may crash, including HTTP Basic and HTTP Digest. Crashes may occur if responses contain server challenges.
*   Cache control through `[CachedResponseHandler](Protocols/CachedResponseHandler.html) ` and associated APIs is unavailable, as the underlying delegate methods aren’t called.
*   `URLSessionTaskMetrics` are never gathered.
*   `WebSocketRequest` is not available.

Due to these issues, Alamofire is unsupported on Linux, Windows, and Android. Please report any crashes to the [Swift bug reporter](https://bugs.swift.org)
.

Communication
-------------

*   If you **need help with making network requests** using Alamofire, use [Stack Overflow](https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/alamofire)
     and tag `alamofire`.
*   If you need to **find or understand an API**, check [our documentation](http://alamofire.github.io/Alamofire/)
     or [Apple’s documentation for `URLSession`](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/foundation/url_loading_system)
    , on top of which Alamofire is built.
*   If you need **help with an Alamofire feature**, use [our forum on swift.org](https://forums.swift.org/c/related-projects/alamofire)
    .
*   If you’d like to **discuss Alamofire best practices**, use [our forum on swift.org](https://forums.swift.org/c/related-projects/alamofire)
    .
*   If you’d like to **discuss a feature request**, use [our forum on swift.org](https://forums.swift.org/c/related-projects/alamofire)
    .
*   If you **found a bug**, open an issue here on GitHub and follow the guide. The more detail the better!

Installation
------------

### Swift Package Manager

The [Swift Package Manager](https://swift.org/package-manager/)
 is a tool for automating the distribution of Swift code and is integrated into the `swift` compiler.

Once you have your Swift package set up, adding Alamofire as a dependency is as easy as adding it to the `dependencies` value of your `Package.swift` or the Package list in Xcode.

    dependencies: [\
        .package(url: "https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire.git", .upToNextMajor(from: "5.10.0"))\
    ]
    

Normally you’ll want to depend on the `Alamofire` target:

    .product(name: "Alamofire", package: "Alamofire")
    

But if you want to force Alamofire to be dynamically linked (do not do this unless you’re sure you need it), you can depend on the `AlamofireDynamic` target:

    .product(name: "AlamofireDynamic", package: "Alamofire")
    

### CocoaPods

[CocoaPods](https://cocoapods.org)
 is a dependency manager for Cocoa projects. For usage and installation instructions, visit their website. To integrate Alamofire into your Xcode project using CocoaPods, specify it in your `Podfile`:

    pod 'Alamofire'
    

### Carthage

[Carthage](https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage)
 is a decentralized dependency manager that builds your dependencies and provides you with binary frameworks. To integrate Alamofire into your Xcode project using Carthage, specify it in your `Cartfile`:

    github "Alamofire/Alamofire"
    

### Manually

If you prefer not to use any of the aforementioned dependency managers, you can integrate Alamofire into your project manually.

#### Embedded Framework

*   Open up Terminal, `cd` into your top-level project directory, and run the following command “if” your project is not initialized as a git repository:

      $ git init
    

*   Add Alamofire as a git [submodule](https://git-scm.com/docs/git-submodule)
     by running the following command:

      $ git submodule add https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire.git
    

*   Open the new `Alamofire` folder, and drag the `Alamofire.xcodeproj` into the Project Navigator of your application’s Xcode project.

> It should appear nested underneath your application’s blue project icon. Whether it is above or below all the other Xcode groups does not matter.

*   Select the `Alamofire.xcodeproj` in the Project Navigator and verify the deployment target matches that of your application target.
*   Next, select your application project in the Project Navigator (blue project icon) to navigate to the target configuration window and select the application target under the “Targets” heading in the sidebar.
*   In the tab bar at the top of that window, open the “General” panel.
*   Click on the `+` button under the “Embedded Binaries” section.
*   You will see two different `Alamofire.xcodeproj` folders each with two different versions of the `Alamofire.framework` nested inside a `Products` folder.

> It does not matter which `Products` folder you choose from, but it does matter whether you choose the top or bottom `Alamofire.framework`.

*   Select the top `Alamofire.framework` for iOS and the bottom one for macOS.

> You can verify which one you selected by inspecting the build log for your project. The build target for `Alamofire` will be listed as `Alamofire iOS`, `Alamofire macOS`, `Alamofire tvOS`, or `Alamofire watchOS`.

*   And that’s it!

> The `Alamofire.framework` is automagically added as a target dependency, linked framework and embedded framework in a copy files build phase which is all you need to build on the simulator and a device.

Contributing
------------

Before contributing to Alamofire, please read the instructions detailed in our [contribution guide](https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md)
.

Open Radars
-----------

The following radars have some effect on the current implementation of Alamofire.

*   [`rdar://21349340`](http://www.openradar.me/radar?id=5517037090635776)
     - Compiler throwing warning due to toll-free bridging issue in the test case
*   `rdar://26870455` - Background URL Session Configurations do not work in the simulator
*   `rdar://26849668` - Some URLProtocol APIs do not properly handle `URLRequest`

Resolved Radars
---------------

The following radars have been resolved over time after being filed against the Alamofire project.

*   [`rdar://26761490`](http://www.openradar.me/radar?id=5010235949318144)
     - Swift string interpolation causing memory leak with common usage.
    *   (Resolved): 9/1/17 in Xcode 9 beta 6.
*   [`rdar://36082113`](http://openradar.appspot.com/radar?id=4942308441063424)
     - `URLSessionTaskMetrics` failing to link on watchOS 3.0+
    *   (Resolved): Just add `CFNetwork` to your linked frameworks.
*   `FB7624529` - `urlSession(_:task:didFinishCollecting:)` never called on watchOS
    *   (Resolved): Metrics now collected on watchOS 7+.

FAQ
---

### What’s the origin of the name Alamofire?

Alamofire is named after the [Alamo Fire flower](https://aggie-horticulture.tamu.edu/wildseed/alamofire.html)
, a hybrid variant of the Bluebonnet, the official state flower of Texas.

Credits
-------

Alamofire is owned and maintained by the [Alamofire Software Foundation](http://alamofire.org)
. You can follow them on Twitter at [@AlamofireSF](https://twitter.com/AlamofireSF)
 for project updates and releases.

### Security Disclosure

If you believe you have identified a security vulnerability with Alamofire, you should report it as soon as possible via email to [security@alamofire.org](mailto:security@alamofire.org)
. Please do not post it to a public issue tracker.

Sponsorship
-----------

The [ASF](https://github.com/Alamofire/Foundation#members)
 is looking to raise money to officially stay registered as a federal non-profit organization. Registering will allow Foundation members to gain some legal protections and also allow us to put donations to use, tax-free. Sponsoring the ASF will enable us to:

*   Pay our yearly legal fees to keep the non-profit in good status
*   Pay for our mail servers to help us stay on top of all questions and security issues
*   Potentially fund test servers to make it easier for us to test the edge cases
*   Potentially fund developers to work on one of our projects full-time

The community adoption of the ASF libraries has been amazing. We are greatly humbled by your enthusiasm around the projects and want to continue to do everything we can to move the needle forward. With your continued support, the ASF will be able to improve its reach and also provide better legal safety for the core members. If you use any of our libraries for work, see if your employers would be interested in donating. Any amount you can donate, whether once or monthly, to help us reach our goal would be greatly appreciated.

[Sponsor Alamofire](https://github.com/sponsors/Alamofire)

Supporters
----------

 provides Alamofire with a free, hosted Mac mini.

# Adapter Class Reference

Adapter
=======

Closure-based `[RequestAdapter](../Protocols/RequestAdapter.html) `.

# Alamofire  Reference

![Alamofire: Elegant Networking in Swift](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Alamofire/Alamofire/master/Resources/AlamofireLogo.png)

[![Swift](https://img.shields.io/badge/Swift-5.9_5.10_6.0-orange?style=flat-square)](https://img.shields.io/badge/Swift-5.9_5.10_6.0-Orange?style=flat-square)
 [![Platforms](https://img.shields.io/badge/Platforms-macOS_iOS_tvOS_watchOS_visionOS_Linux_Windows_Android-yellowgreen?style=flat-square)](https://img.shields.io/badge/Platforms-macOS_iOS_tvOS_watchOS_vision_OS_Linux_Windows_Android-Green?style=flat-square)

Alamofire is an HTTP networking library written in Swift.

Features
--------

*   \[x\] Chainable Request / Response Methods
*   \[x\] Swift Concurrency Support Back to iOS 13, macOS 10.15, tvOS 13, and watchOS 6.
*   \[x\] Combine Support
*   \[x\] URL / JSON Parameter Encoding
*   \[x\] Upload File / Data / Stream / MultipartFormData
*   \[x\] Download File using Request or Resume Data
*   \[x\] Authentication with `URLCredential`
*   \[x\] HTTP Response Validation
*   \[x\] Upload and Download Progress Closures with Progress
*   \[x\] cURL Command Output
*   \[x\] Dynamically Adapt and Retry Requests
*   \[x\] TLS Certificate and Public Key Pinning
*   \[x\] Network Reachability
*   \[x\] Comprehensive Unit and Integration Test Coverage
*   \[x\] [Complete Documentation](https://alamofire.github.io/Alamofire)
    

Write Requests Fast!
--------------------

Alamofire’s compact syntax and extensive feature set allow requests with powerful features like automatic retry to be written in just a few lines of code.

    // Automatic String to URL conversion, Swift concurrency support, and automatic retry.
    let response = await AF.request("https://httpbin.org/get", interceptor: .retryPolicy)
                           // Automatic HTTP Basic Auth.
                           .authenticate(username: "user", password: "pass")
                           // Caching customization.
                           .cacheResponse(using: .cache)
                           // Redirect customization.
                           .redirect(using: .follow)
                           // Validate response code and Content-Type.
                           .validate()
                           // Produce a cURL command for the request.
                           .cURLDescription { description in
                             print(description)
                           }
                           // Automatic Decodable support with background parsing.
                           .serializingDecodable(DecodableType.self)
                           // Await the full response with metrics and a parsed body.
                           .response
    // Detailed response description for easy debugging.
    debugPrint(response)
    

Component Libraries
-------------------

In order to keep Alamofire focused specifically on core networking implementations, additional component libraries have been created by the [Alamofire Software Foundation](https://github.com/Alamofire/Foundation)
 to bring additional functionality to the Alamofire ecosystem.

*   [AlamofireImage](https://github.com/Alamofire/AlamofireImage)
     - An image library including image response serializers, `UIImage` and `UIImageView` extensions, custom image filters, an auto-purging in-memory cache, and a priority-based image downloading system.
*   [AlamofireNetworkActivityIndicator](https://github.com/Alamofire/AlamofireNetworkActivityIndicator)
     - Controls the visibility of the network activity indicator on iOS using Alamofire. It contains configurable delay timers to help mitigate flicker and can support `URLSession` instances not managed by Alamofire.

Requirements
------------

| Platform | Minimum Swift Version | Installation | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| iOS 10.0+ / macOS 10.12+ / tvOS 10.0+ / watchOS 3.0+ | 5.9 / Xcode 15.0 | [CocoaPods](#cocoapods)<br>, [Carthage](#carthage)<br>, [Swift Package Manager](#swift-package-manager)<br>, [Manual](#manually) | Fully Tested |
| Linux | Latest Only | [Swift Package Manager](#swift-package-manager) | Building But Unsupported |
| Windows | Latest Only | [Swift Package Manager](#swift-package-manager) | Building But Unsupported |
| Android | Latest Only | [Swift Package Manager](#swift-package-manager) | Building But Unsupported |

#### Known Issues on Linux and Windows

Alamofire builds on Linux, Windows, and Android but there are missing features and many issues in the underlying `swift-corelibs-foundation` that prevent full functionality and may cause crashes. These include:

*   `[ServerTrustManager](Classes/ServerTrustManager.html) ` and associated certificate functionality is unavailable, so there is no certificate pinning and no client certificate support.
*   Various methods of HTTP authentication may crash, including HTTP Basic and HTTP Digest. Crashes may occur if responses contain server challenges.
*   Cache control through `[CachedResponseHandler](Protocols/CachedResponseHandler.html) ` and associated APIs is unavailable, as the underlying delegate methods aren’t called.
*   `URLSessionTaskMetrics` are never gathered.
*   `WebSocketRequest` is not available.

Due to these issues, Alamofire is unsupported on Linux, Windows, and Android. Please report any crashes to the [Swift bug reporter](https://bugs.swift.org)
.

Communication
-------------

*   If you **need help with making network requests** using Alamofire, use [Stack Overflow](https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/alamofire)
     and tag `alamofire`.
*   If you need to **find or understand an API**, check [our documentation](http://alamofire.github.io/Alamofire/)
     or [Apple’s documentation for `URLSession`](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/foundation/url_loading_system)
    , on top of which Alamofire is built.
*   If you need **help with an Alamofire feature**, use [our forum on swift.org](https://forums.swift.org/c/related-projects/alamofire)
    .
*   If you’d like to **discuss Alamofire best practices**, use [our forum on swift.org](https://forums.swift.org/c/related-projects/alamofire)
    .
*   If you’d like to **discuss a feature request**, use [our forum on swift.org](https://forums.swift.org/c/related-projects/alamofire)
    .
*   If you **found a bug**, open an issue here on GitHub and follow the guide. The more detail the better!

Installation
------------

### Swift Package Manager

The [Swift Package Manager](https://swift.org/package-manager/)
 is a tool for automating the distribution of Swift code and is integrated into the `swift` compiler.

Once you have your Swift package set up, adding Alamofire as a dependency is as easy as adding it to the `dependencies` value of your `Package.swift` or the Package list in Xcode.

    dependencies: [\
        .package(url: "https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire.git", .upToNextMajor(from: "5.10.0"))\
    ]
    

Normally you’ll want to depend on the `Alamofire` target:

    .product(name: "Alamofire", package: "Alamofire")
    

But if you want to force Alamofire to be dynamically linked (do not do this unless you’re sure you need it), you can depend on the `AlamofireDynamic` target:

    .product(name: "AlamofireDynamic", package: "Alamofire")
    

### CocoaPods

[CocoaPods](https://cocoapods.org)
 is a dependency manager for Cocoa projects. For usage and installation instructions, visit their website. To integrate Alamofire into your Xcode project using CocoaPods, specify it in your `Podfile`:

    pod 'Alamofire'
    

### Carthage

[Carthage](https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage)
 is a decentralized dependency manager that builds your dependencies and provides you with binary frameworks. To integrate Alamofire into your Xcode project using Carthage, specify it in your `Cartfile`:

    github "Alamofire/Alamofire"
    

### Manually

If you prefer not to use any of the aforementioned dependency managers, you can integrate Alamofire into your project manually.

#### Embedded Framework

*   Open up Terminal, `cd` into your top-level project directory, and run the following command “if” your project is not initialized as a git repository:

      $ git init
    

*   Add Alamofire as a git [submodule](https://git-scm.com/docs/git-submodule)
     by running the following command:

      $ git submodule add https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire.git
    

*   Open the new `Alamofire` folder, and drag the `Alamofire.xcodeproj` into the Project Navigator of your application’s Xcode project.

> It should appear nested underneath your application’s blue project icon. Whether it is above or below all the other Xcode groups does not matter.

*   Select the `Alamofire.xcodeproj` in the Project Navigator and verify the deployment target matches that of your application target.
*   Next, select your application project in the Project Navigator (blue project icon) to navigate to the target configuration window and select the application target under the “Targets” heading in the sidebar.
*   In the tab bar at the top of that window, open the “General” panel.
*   Click on the `+` button under the “Embedded Binaries” section.
*   You will see two different `Alamofire.xcodeproj` folders each with two different versions of the `Alamofire.framework` nested inside a `Products` folder.

> It does not matter which `Products` folder you choose from, but it does matter whether you choose the top or bottom `Alamofire.framework`.

*   Select the top `Alamofire.framework` for iOS and the bottom one for macOS.

> You can verify which one you selected by inspecting the build log for your project. The build target for `Alamofire` will be listed as `Alamofire iOS`, `Alamofire macOS`, `Alamofire tvOS`, or `Alamofire watchOS`.

*   And that’s it!

> The `Alamofire.framework` is automagically added as a target dependency, linked framework and embedded framework in a copy files build phase which is all you need to build on the simulator and a device.

Contributing
------------

Before contributing to Alamofire, please read the instructions detailed in our [contribution guide](https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md)
.

Open Radars
-----------

The following radars have some effect on the current implementation of Alamofire.

*   [`rdar://21349340`](http://www.openradar.me/radar?id=5517037090635776)
     - Compiler throwing warning due to toll-free bridging issue in the test case
*   `rdar://26870455` - Background URL Session Configurations do not work in the simulator
*   `rdar://26849668` - Some URLProtocol APIs do not properly handle `URLRequest`

Resolved Radars
---------------

The following radars have been resolved over time after being filed against the Alamofire project.

*   [`rdar://26761490`](http://www.openradar.me/radar?id=5010235949318144)
     - Swift string interpolation causing memory leak with common usage.
    *   (Resolved): 9/1/17 in Xcode 9 beta 6.
*   [`rdar://36082113`](http://openradar.appspot.com/radar?id=4942308441063424)
     - `URLSessionTaskMetrics` failing to link on watchOS 3.0+
    *   (Resolved): Just add `CFNetwork` to your linked frameworks.
*   `FB7624529` - `urlSession(_:task:didFinishCollecting:)` never called on watchOS
    *   (Resolved): Metrics now collected on watchOS 7+.

FAQ
---

### What’s the origin of the name Alamofire?

Alamofire is named after the [Alamo Fire flower](https://aggie-horticulture.tamu.edu/wildseed/alamofire.html)
, a hybrid variant of the Bluebonnet, the official state flower of Texas.

Credits
-------

Alamofire is owned and maintained by the [Alamofire Software Foundation](http://alamofire.org)
. You can follow them on Twitter at [@AlamofireSF](https://twitter.com/AlamofireSF)
 for project updates and releases.

### Security Disclosure

If you believe you have identified a security vulnerability with Alamofire, you should report it as soon as possible via email to [security@alamofire.org](mailto:security@alamofire.org)
. Please do not post it to a public issue tracker.

Sponsorship
-----------

The [ASF](https://github.com/Alamofire/Foundation#members)
 is looking to raise money to officially stay registered as a federal non-profit organization. Registering will allow Foundation members to gain some legal protections and also allow us to put donations to use, tax-free. Sponsoring the ASF will enable us to:

*   Pay our yearly legal fees to keep the non-profit in good status
*   Pay for our mail servers to help us stay on top of all questions and security issues
*   Potentially fund test servers to make it easier for us to test the edge cases
*   Potentially fund developers to work on one of our projects full-time

The community adoption of the ASF libraries has been amazing. We are greatly humbled by your enthusiasm around the projects and want to continue to do everything we can to move the needle forward. With your continued support, the ASF will be able to improve its reach and also provide better legal safety for the core members. If you use any of our libraries for work, see if your employers would be interested in donating. Any amount you can donate, whether once or monthly, to help us reach our goal would be greatly appreciated.

[Sponsor Alamofire](https://github.com/sponsors/Alamofire)

# Classes  Reference

Classes
=======

The following classes are available globally.

*   `[DataRequest](#/s:9Alamofire11DataRequestC) `
    
    `[Request](Classes/Request.html) ` subclass which handles in-memory `Data` download using `URLSessionDataTask`.
    
    [See more](Classes/DataRequest.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DataStreamRequest](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC) `
    
    `[Request](Classes/Request.html) ` subclass which streams HTTP response `Data` through a `Handler` closure.
    
    [See more](Classes/DataStreamRequest.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DownloadRequest](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC) `
    
    `[Request](Classes/Request.html) ` subclass which downloads `Data` to a file on disk using `URLSessionDownloadTask`.
    
    [See more](Classes/DownloadRequest.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Request](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC) `
    
    `Request` is the common superclass of all Alamofire request types and provides common state, delegate, and callback handling.
    
    [See more](Classes/Request.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[AlamofireNotifications](#/s:9Alamofire0A13NotificationsC) `
    
    `[EventMonitor](Protocols/EventMonitor.html) ` that provides Alamofire’s notifications.
    
    [See more](Classes/AlamofireNotifications.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[JSONParameterEncoder](#/s:9Alamofire20JSONParameterEncoderC) `
    
    A `[ParameterEncoder](Protocols/ParameterEncoder.html) ` that encodes types as JSON body data.
    
    If no `Content-Type` header is already set on the provided `URLRequest`s, it’s set to `application/json`.
    
    [See more](Classes/JSONParameterEncoder.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC) `
    
    A `[ParameterEncoder](Protocols/ParameterEncoder.html) ` that encodes types as URL-encoded query strings to be set on the URL or as body data, depending on the `Destination` set.
    
    If no `Content-Type` header is already set on the provided `URLRequest`s, it will be set to `application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8`.
    
    Encoding behavior can be customized by passing an instance of `[URLEncodedFormEncoder](Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder.html) ` to the initializer.
    
    [See more](Classes/URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Session](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC) `
    
    `Session` creates and manages Alamofire’s `[Request](Classes/Request.html) ` types during their lifetimes. It also provides common functionality for all `[Request](Classes/Request.html) `s, including queuing, interception, trust management, redirect handling, and response cache handling.
    
    [See more](Classes/Session.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[SessionDelegate](#/c:@M@Alamofire@objc(cs)SessionDelegate) `
    
    Class which implements the various `URLSessionDelegate` methods to connect various Alamofire features.
    
    [See more](Classes/SessionDelegate.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[UploadRequest](#/s:9Alamofire13UploadRequestC) `
    
    `[DataRequest](Classes/DataRequest.html) ` subclass which handles `Data` upload from memory, file, or stream using `URLSessionUploadTask`.
    
    [See more](Classes/UploadRequest.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[AuthenticationInterceptor](#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC) `
    
    The `AuthenticationInterceptor` class manages the queuing and threading complexity of authenticating requests. It relies on an `[Authenticator](Protocols/Authenticator.html) ` type to handle the actual `URLRequest` authentication and `Credential` refresh.
    
    [See more](Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[CompositeEventMonitor](#/s:9Alamofire21CompositeEventMonitorC) `
    
    An `[EventMonitor](Protocols/EventMonitor.html) ` which can contain multiple `[EventMonitor](Protocols/EventMonitor.html) `s and calls their methods on their queues.
    
    [See more](Classes/CompositeEventMonitor.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ClosureEventMonitor](#/s:9Alamofire19ClosureEventMonitorC) `
    
    `[EventMonitor](Protocols/EventMonitor.html) ` that allows optional closures to be set to receive events.
    
    [See more](Classes/ClosureEventMonitor.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[MultipartFormData](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC) `
    
    Constructs `multipart/form-data` for uploads within an HTTP or HTTPS body. There are currently two ways to encode multipart form data. The first way is to encode the data directly in memory. This is very efficient, but can lead to memory issues if the dataset is too large. The second way is designed for larger datasets and will write all the data to a single file on disk with all the proper boundary segmentation. The second approach MUST be used for larger datasets such as video content, otherwise your app may run out of memory when trying to encode the dataset.
    
    For more information on `multipart/form-data` in general, please refer to the RFC-2388 and RFC-2045 specs as well and the w3 form documentation.
    
    *   [https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2388.txt](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2388.txt)
        
    *   [https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2045.txt](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2045.txt)
        
    *   [https://www.w3.org/TR/html401/interact/forms.html#h-17.13](https://www.w3.org/TR/html401/interact/forms.html#h-17.13)
        
    
    [See more](Classes/MultipartFormData.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[NetworkReachabilityManager](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC) `
    
    The `NetworkReachabilityManager` class listens for reachability changes of hosts and addresses for both cellular and WiFi network interfaces.
    
    Reachability can be used to determine background information about why a network operation failed, or to retry network requests when a connection is established. It should not be used to prevent a user from initiating a network request, as it’s possible that an initial request may be required to establish reachability.
    
    [See more](Classes/NetworkReachabilityManager.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Adapter](#/s:9Alamofire7AdapterC) `
    
    Closure-based `[RequestAdapter](Protocols/RequestAdapter.html) `.
    
    [See more](Classes/Adapter.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Retrier](#/s:9Alamofire7RetrierC) `
    
    Closure-based `[RequestRetrier](Protocols/RequestRetrier.html) `.
    
    [See more](Classes/Retrier.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Interceptor](#/s:9Alamofire11InterceptorC) `

    [See more](Classes/Interceptor.html)

[](#/Data)

### Data

*   `[DataResponseSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire22DataResponseSerializerC) `
    
    A `[ResponseSerializer](Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` that performs minimal response checking and returns any response `Data` as-is. By default, a request returning `nil` or no data is considered an error. However, if the request has an `[HTTPMethod](Structs/HTTPMethod.html) ` or the response has an HTTP status code valid for empty responses, then an empty `Data` value is returned.
    
    [See more](Classes/DataResponseSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/String)

### String

*   `[StringResponseSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire24StringResponseSerializerC) `
    
    A `[ResponseSerializer](Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` that decodes the response data as a `String`. By default, a request returning `nil` or no data is considered an error. However, if the request has an `[HTTPMethod](Structs/HTTPMethod.html) ` or the response has an HTTP status code valid for empty responses, then an empty `String` is returned.
    
    [See more](Classes/StringResponseSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/JSON)

### JSON

*   `[JSONResponseSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire22JSONResponseSerializerC) `
    
    A `[ResponseSerializer](Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` that decodes the response data using `JSONSerialization`. By default, a request returning `nil` or no data is considered an error. However, if the request has an `[HTTPMethod](Structs/HTTPMethod.html) ` or the response has an HTTP status code valid for empty responses, then an `NSNull` value is returned.
    
    [See more](Classes/JSONResponseSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Decodable)

### Decodable

*   `[DecodableResponseSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire27DecodableResponseSerializerC) `
    
    A `[ResponseSerializer](Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` that decodes the response data as a `Decodable` value using any decoder that conforms to `[DataDecoder](Protocols/DataDecoder.html) `. By default, this is an instance of `JSONDecoder`.
    
    [See more](Classes/DecodableResponseSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[RetryPolicy](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC) `
    
    A retry policy that retries requests using an exponential backoff for allowed HTTP methods and HTTP status codes as well as certain types of networking errors.
    
    [See more](Classes/RetryPolicy.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

*   `[ConnectionLostRetryPolicy](#/s:9Alamofire25ConnectionLostRetryPolicyC) `
    
    A retry policy that automatically retries idempotent requests for network connection lost errors. For more information about retrying network connection lost errors, please refer to Apple’s [technical document](https://developer.apple.com/library/content/qa/qa1941/_index.html)
    .
    
    [See more](Classes/ConnectionLostRetryPolicy.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ServerTrustManager](#/s:9Alamofire18ServerTrustManagerC) `
    
    Responsible for managing the mapping of `[ServerTrustEvaluating](Protocols/ServerTrustEvaluating.html) ` values to given hosts.
    
    [See more](Classes/ServerTrustManager.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Server%20Trust%20Evaluators)

### Server Trust Evaluators

*   `[DefaultTrustEvaluator](#/s:9Alamofire21DefaultTrustEvaluatorC) `
    
    An evaluator which uses the default server trust evaluation while allowing you to control whether to validate the host provided by the challenge. Applications are encouraged to always validate the host in production environments to guarantee the validity of the server’s certificate chain.
    
    [See more](Classes/DefaultTrustEvaluator.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[RevocationTrustEvaluator](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC) `
    
    An evaluator which Uses the default and revoked server trust evaluations allowing you to control whether to validate the host provided by the challenge as well as specify the revocation flags for testing for revoked certificates. Apple platforms did not start testing for revoked certificates automatically until iOS 10.1, macOS 10.12 and tvOS 10.1 which is demonstrated in our TLS tests. Applications are encouraged to always validate the host in production environments to guarantee the validity of the server’s certificate chain.
    
    [See more](Classes/RevocationTrustEvaluator.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator](#/s:9Alamofire32PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluatorC) `
    
    Uses the pinned certificates to validate the server trust. The server trust is considered valid if one of the pinned certificates match one of the server certificates. By validating both the certificate chain and host, certificate pinning provides a very secure form of server trust validation mitigating most, if not all, MITM attacks. Applications are encouraged to always validate the host and require a valid certificate chain in production environments.
    
    [See more](Classes/PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[PublicKeysTrustEvaluator](#/s:9Alamofire24PublicKeysTrustEvaluatorC) `
    
    Uses the pinned public keys to validate the server trust. The server trust is considered valid if one of the pinned public keys match one of the server certificate public keys. By validating both the certificate chain and host, public key pinning provides a very secure form of server trust validation mitigating most, if not all, MITM attacks. Applications are encouraged to always validate the host and require a valid certificate chain in production environments.
    
    [See more](Classes/PublicKeysTrustEvaluator.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[CompositeTrustEvaluator](#/s:9Alamofire23CompositeTrustEvaluatorC) `
    
    Uses the provided evaluators to validate the server trust. The trust is only considered valid if all of the evaluators consider it valid.
    
    [See more](Classes/CompositeTrustEvaluator.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DisabledTrustEvaluator](#/s:9Alamofire22DisabledTrustEvaluatorC) `
    
    Disables all evaluation which in turn will always consider any server trust as valid.
    
    **THIS EVALUATOR SHOULD NEVER BE USED IN PRODUCTION!**
    
    [See more](Classes/DisabledTrustEvaluator.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[URLEncodedFormEncoder](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC) `
    
    An object that encodes instances into URL-encoded query strings.
    
    `ArrayEncoding` can be used to configure how `Array` values are encoded. By default, the `.brackets` encoding is used, encoding array values with brackets for each value. e.g `array[]=1&array[]=2`.
    
    `BoolEncoding` can be used to configure how `Bool` values are encoded. By default, the `.numeric` encoding is used, encoding `true` as `1` and `false` as `0`.
    
    `DataEncoding` can be used to configure how `Data` values are encoded. By default, the `.deferredToData` encoding is used, which encodes `Data` values using their default `Encodable` implementation.
    
    `DateEncoding` can be used to configure how `Date` values are encoded. By default, the `.deferredToDate` encoding is used, which encodes `Date`s using their default `Encodable` implementation.
    
    `KeyEncoding` can be used to configure how keys are encoded. By default, the `.useDefaultKeys` encoding is used, which encodes the keys directly from the `Encodable` implementation.
    
    `KeyPathEncoding` can be used to configure how paths within nested objects are encoded. By default, the `.brackets` encoding is used, which encodes each sub-key in brackets. e.g. `parent[child][grandchild]=value`.
    
    `NilEncoding` can be used to configure how `nil` `Optional` values are encoded. By default, the `.dropKey` encoding is used, which drops `nil` key / value pairs from the output entirely.
    
    `SpaceEncoding` can be used to configure how spaces are encoded. By default, the `.percentEscaped` encoding is used, replacing spaces with `%20`.
    
    This type is largely based on Vapor’s [`url-encoded-form`](https://github.com/vapor/url-encoded-form)
     project.
    
    [See more](Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder.html)
    
    #### Declaration

---

# AuthenticationInterceptor Class Reference

AuthenticationInterceptor
=========================

The `AuthenticationInterceptor` class manages the queuing and threading complexity of authenticating requests. It relies on an `[Authenticator](../Protocols/Authenticator.html) ` type to handle the actual `URLRequest` authentication and `Credential` refresh.

[](#/Typealiases)

### Typealiases

*   `[Credential](#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC10Credentiala) `
    
    Type of credential used to authenticate requests.
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Helper%20Types)

### Helper Types

*   `[RefreshWindow](#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV) `
    
    Type that defines a time window used to identify excessive refresh calls. When enabled, prior to executing a refresh, the `[AuthenticationInterceptor](../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor.html) ` compares the timestamp history of previous refresh calls against the `RefreshWindow`. If more refreshes have occurred within the refresh window than allowed, the refresh is cancelled and an `AuthorizationError.excessiveRefresh` error is thrown.
    
    [See more](../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Properties)

### Properties

*   `[credential](#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC10credential10CredentialQzSgvp) `
    
    The `[Credential](../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor.html#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC10Credentiala) ` used to authenticate requests.
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Initialization)

### Initialization

*   `[init(authenticator:credential:refreshWindow:)](#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13authenticator10credential13refreshWindowACyxGx_10CredentialQzSgAC07RefreshG0Vyx_GSgtcfc) `
    
    Creates an `AuthenticationInterceptor` instance from the specified parameters.
    
    A `nil` `[RefreshWindow](../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html) ` will result in the `AuthenticationInterceptor` not checking for excessive refresh calls. It is recommended to always use a `[RefreshWindow](../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html) ` to avoid endless refresh cycles.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_authenticator_` | The `[Authenticator](../Protocols/Authenticator.html) ` type. |
    | `_credential_` | The `[Credential](../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor.html#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC10Credentiala) ` if it exists. `nil` by default. |
    | `_refreshWindow_` | The `[RefreshWindow](../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html) ` used to identify excessive refresh calls. `RefreshWindow()` by default. |
    

[](#/Adapt)

### Adapt

*   `[adapt(_:for:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestAdapterP5adapt_3for10completiony10Foundation10URLRequestV_AA7SessionCys6ResultOyAIs5Error_pGYbctF) `

# RefreshWindow Structure Reference

RefreshWindow
=============

Type that defines a time window used to identify excessive refresh calls. When enabled, prior to executing a refresh, the `[AuthenticationInterceptor](../../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor.html) ` compares the timestamp history of previous refresh calls against the `RefreshWindow`. If more refreshes have occurred within the refresh window than allowed, the refresh is cancelled and an `AuthorizationError.excessiveRefresh` error is thrown.

*   `[interval](#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV8intervalSdvp) `
    
    `TimeInterval` defining the duration of the time window before the current time in which the number of refresh attempts is compared against `[maximumAttempts](../../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV15maximumAttemptsSivp) `. For example, if `interval` is 30 seconds, then the `RefreshWindow` represents the past 30 seconds. If more attempts occurred in the past 30 seconds than `[maximumAttempts](../../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV15maximumAttemptsSivp) `, an `.excessiveRefresh` error will be thrown.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[maximumAttempts](#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV15maximumAttemptsSivp) `
    
    Total refresh attempts allowed within `[interval](../../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV8intervalSdvp) ` before throwing an `.excessiveRefresh` error.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(interval:maximumAttempts:)](#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV8interval15maximumAttemptsAEyx_GSd_Sitcfc) `
    
    Creates a `RefreshWindow` instance from the specified `[interval](../../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV8intervalSdvp) ` and `[maximumAttempts](../../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor/RefreshWindow.html#/s:9Alamofire25AuthenticationInterceptorC13RefreshWindowV15maximumAttemptsSivp) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_interval_` | `TimeInterval` defining the duration of the time window before the current time. |
    | `_maximumAttempts_` | The maximum attempts allowed within the `TimeInterval`. |

---

# CompositeTrustEvaluator Class Reference

CompositeTrustEvaluator
=======================

Uses the provided evaluators to validate the server trust. The trust is only considered valid if all of the evaluators consider it valid.

*   `[init(evaluators:)](#/s:9Alamofire23CompositeTrustEvaluatorC10evaluatorsACSayAA06ServerC10Evaluating_pG_tcfc) `
    
    Creates a `CompositeTrustEvaluator` from the provided evaluators.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_evaluators_` | The `[ServerTrustEvaluating](../Protocols/ServerTrustEvaluating.html) ` values used to evaluate the server trust. |
    
*   `[evaluate(_:forHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingP8evaluate_7forHostySo03SecC3Refa_SStKF) `

# ConnectionLostRetryPolicy Class Reference

ConnectionLostRetryPolicy
=========================

A retry policy that automatically retries idempotent requests for network connection lost errors. For more information about retrying network connection lost errors, please refer to Apple’s [technical document](https://developer.apple.com/library/content/qa/qa1941/_index.html)
.

*   `[init(retryLimit:exponentialBackoffBase:exponentialBackoffScale:retryableHTTPMethods:)](#/s:9Alamofire25ConnectionLostRetryPolicyC10retryLimit22exponentialBackoffBase0hI5Scale20retryableHTTPMethodsACSu_SuSdShyAA10HTTPMethodVGtcfc) `
    
    Creates a `ConnectionLostRetryPolicy` instance from the specified parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_retryLimit_` | The total number of times the request is allowed to be retried. `[RetryPolicy.defaultRetryLimit](../Classes/RetryPolicy.html#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC07defaultB5LimitSuvpZ) ` by default. |
    | `_exponentialBackoffBase_` | The base of the exponential backoff policy. `[RetryPolicy.defaultExponentialBackoffBase](../Classes/RetryPolicy.html#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC29defaultExponentialBackoffBaseSuvpZ) ` by default. |
    | `_exponentialBackoffScale_` | The scale of the exponential backoff. `[RetryPolicy.defaultExponentialBackoffScale](../Classes/RetryPolicy.html#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC30defaultExponentialBackoffScaleSdvpZ) ` by default. |
    | `_retryableHTTPMethods_` | The idempotent http methods to retry. `[RetryPolicy.defaultRetryableHTTPMethods](../Classes/RetryPolicy.html#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC27defaultRetryableHTTPMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvpZ) ` by default. |

---

# DataResponseSerializer Class Reference

DataResponseSerializer
======================

A `[ResponseSerializer](../Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` that performs minimal response checking and returns any response `Data` as-is. By default, a request returning `nil` or no data is considered an error. However, if the request has an `[HTTPMethod](../Structs/HTTPMethod.html) ` or the response has an HTTP status code valid for empty responses, then an empty `Data` value is returned.

*   `[dataPreprocessor](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP16dataPreprocessorAA04DataE0_pvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[emptyResponseCodes](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP05emptyB5CodesShySiGvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[emptyRequestMethods](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP19emptyRequestMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(dataPreprocessor:emptyResponseCodes:emptyRequestMethods:)](#/s:9Alamofire22DataResponseSerializerC16dataPreprocessor05emptyC5Codes0G14RequestMethodsAcA0bF0_p_ShySiGShyAA10HTTPMethodVGtcfc) `
    
    Creates a `DataResponseSerializer` using the provided parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_dataPreprocessor_` | `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) ` used to prepare the received `Data` for serialization. |
    | `_emptyResponseCodes_` | The HTTP response codes for which empty responses are allowed. `[204, 205]` by default. |
    | `_emptyRequestMethods_` | The HTTP request methods for which empty responses are allowed. `[.head]` by default. |
    
*   `[serialize(request:response:data:error:)](#/s:9Alamofire30DataResponseSerializerProtocolP9serialize7request8response4data5error16SerializedObjectQz10Foundation10URLRequestVSg_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgAK0B0VSgs5Error_pSgtKF) `
    
    #### Declaration

---

# CompositeEventMonitor Class Reference

# Stream Structure Reference

Stream
======

Type encapsulating an `[Event](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Event.html) ` as it flows through the stream, as well as a `[CancellationToken](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest/CancellationToken.html) ` which can be used to stop the stream at any time.

*   `[event](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC0C0V5eventAC5EventOy_xq_Gvp) `
    
    Latest `[Event](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Event.html) ` from the stream.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[token](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC0C0V5tokenAC17CancellationTokenVvp) `
    
    Token used to cancel the stream.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[cancel()](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC0C0V6cancelyyF) `
    
    Cancel the ongoing stream by canceling the underlying `[DataStreamRequest](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[result](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC0C0V6results6ResultOyxq_GSgvp) `
    
    Incoming `Result` values from `Event.stream`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[value](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC0C0V5valuexSgvp) `
    
    `Success` value of the instance, if any.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[error](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC0C0V5errorq_Sgvp) `
    
    `Failure` value of the instance, if any.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[completion](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC0C0V10completionAC10CompletionVSgvp) `
    
    `[Completion](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Completion.html) ` value of the instance, if any.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# DataStreamRequest Class Reference

DataStreamRequest
=================

`[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` subclass which streams HTTP response `Data` through a `Handler` closure.

*   `[Handler](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC7Handlera) `
    
    Closure type handling `[DataStreamRequest.Stream](../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Stream.html) ` values.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Stream](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC0C0V) `
    
    Type encapsulating an `[Event](../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Event.html) ` as it flows through the stream, as well as a `[CancellationToken](../Classes/DataStreamRequest/CancellationToken.html) ` which can be used to stop the stream at any time.
    
    [See more](../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Stream.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Event](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC5EventO) `
    
    Type representing an event flowing through the stream. Contains either the `Result` of processing streamed `Data` or the completion of the stream.
    
    [See more](../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Event.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Completion](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC10CompletionV) `
    
    Value containing the state of a `[DataStreamRequest](../Classes/DataStreamRequest.html) ` when the stream was completed.
    
    [See more](../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Completion.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[CancellationToken](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC17CancellationTokenV) `
    
    Type used to cancel an ongoing stream.
    
    [See more](../Classes/DataStreamRequest/CancellationToken.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[convertible](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC11convertibleAA21URLRequestConvertible_pvp) `
    
    `[URLRequestConvertible](../Protocols/URLRequestConvertible.html) ` value used to create `URLRequest`s for this instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[automaticallyCancelOnStreamError](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC021automaticallyCancelOnC5ErrorSbvp) `
    
    Whether or not the instance will be cancelled if stream parsing encounters an error.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[validate(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC8validateyACXDs6ResultOyyts5Error_pG10Foundation10URLRequestVSg_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCtYbcF) `
    
    Validates the `URLRequest` and `HTTPURLResponse` received for the instance using the provided `[Validation](../Classes/DataStreamRequest.html#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC10Validationa) ` closure.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_validation_` | `[Validation](../Classes/DataStreamRequest.html#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC10Validationa) ` closure used to validate the request and response. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `DataStreamRequest`.
    
*   `[asInputStream(bufferSize:)](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC07asInputC010bufferSizeSo07NSInputC0CSgSi_tF) `
    
    Produces an `InputStream` that receives the `Data` received by the instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_bufferSize_` | Size, in bytes, of the buffer between the `OutputStream` and `InputStream`. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `InputStream` bound to the internal `OutboundStream`.
    
*   `[onHTTPResponse(on:perform:)](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC14onHTTPResponse0E07performACXDSo17OS_dispatch_queueC_ySo17NSHTTPURLResponseC_yAA0D0C19ResponseDispositionOctctF) `
    
    Sets a closure called whenever the `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) ` produces an `HTTPURLResponse` and providing a completion handler to return a `ResponseDisposition` value.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_queue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which the closure will be called. `.main` by default. |
    | `_handler_` | Closure called when the instance produces an `HTTPURLResponse`. The `completionHandler` provided MUST be called, otherwise the request will never complete. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The instance.
    
*   `[onHTTPResponse(on:perform:)](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC14onHTTPResponse0E07performACXDSo17OS_dispatch_queueC_ySo17NSHTTPURLResponseCctF) `

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_queue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which the closure will be called. `.main` by default. |
    | `_handler_` | Closure called when the instance produces an `HTTPURLResponse`. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The instance.

*   `[onHTTPResponse(perform:)](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC14onHTTPResponse7performACXDAA0D0C19ResponseDispositionOSo17NSHTTPURLResponseCYaYbc_tF) `
    
    Sets an async closure returning a `[Request.ResponseDisposition](../Classes/Request/ResponseDisposition.html) `, called whenever the `DataStreamRequest` produces an `HTTPURLResponse`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_handler_` | Async closure executed when a new `HTTPURLResponse` is received and returning a `ResponseDisposition` value. This value determines whether to continue the request or cancel it as if `cancel()` had been called on the instance. Note, this closure is called on an arbitrary thread, so any synchronous calls in it will execute in that context. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The instance.
    
*   `[onHTTPResponse(perform:)](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC14onHTTPResponse7performACXDySo17NSHTTPURLResponseCYaYbc_tF) `

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_handler_` | Async closure executed when a new `HTTPURLResponse` is received. Note, this closure is called on an arbitrary thread, so any synchronous calls in it will execute in that context. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The instance.

*   `[validate()](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC8validateACXDyF) `
    
    Validates that the response has a status code in the default acceptable range of 200…299, and that the content type matches any specified in the Accept HTTP header field.
    
    If validation fails, subsequent calls to response handlers will have an associated error.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The instance.

# Completion Structure Reference

Completion
==========

Value containing the state of a `[DataStreamRequest](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest.html) ` when the stream was completed.

*   `[request](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC10CompletionV7request10Foundation10URLRequestVSgvp) `
    
    Last `URLRequest` issued by the instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[response](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC10CompletionV8responseSo17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgvp) `
    
    Last `HTTPURLResponse` received by the instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[metrics](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC10CompletionV7metricsSo23NSURLSessionTaskMetricsCSgvp) `
    
    Last `URLSessionTaskMetrics` produced for the instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[error](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC10CompletionV5errorAA7AFErrorOSgvp) `
    
    `[AFError](../../Enums/AFError.html) ` produced for the instance, if any.
    
    #### Declaration

# Event Enumeration Reference

Event
=====

Type representing an event flowing through the stream. Contains either the `Result` of processing streamed `Data` or the completion of the stream.

*   `[stream(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC5EventO6streamyAEy_xq_Gs6ResultOyxq_GcAGms8SendableRzs5ErrorR_r0_lF) `
    
    Output produced every time the instance receives additional `Data`. The associated value contains the `Result` of processing the incoming `Data`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[complete(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC5EventO8completeyAEy_xq_GAC10CompletionVcAGms8SendableRzs5ErrorR_r0_lF) `
    
    Output produced when the instance has completed, whether due to stream end, cancellation, or an error. Associated `[Completion](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest/Completion.html) ` value contains the final state.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# CancellationToken Structure Reference

CancellationToken
=================

Type used to cancel an ongoing stream.

*   `[cancel()](#/s:9Alamofire17DataStreamRequestC17CancellationTokenV6cancelyyF) `
    
    Cancel the ongoing stream by canceling the underlying `[DataStreamRequest](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# DataRequest Class Reference

DataRequest
===========

`[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` subclass which handles in-memory `Data` download using `URLSessionDataTask`.

*   `[convertible](#/s:9Alamofire11DataRequestC11convertibleAA21URLRequestConvertible_pvp) `
    
    `[URLRequestConvertible](../Protocols/URLRequestConvertible.html) ` value used to create `URLRequest`s for this instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[data](#/s:9Alamofire11DataRequestC4data10Foundation0B0VSgvp) `
    
    `Data` read from the server so far.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[validate(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire11DataRequestC8validateyACXDs6ResultOyyts5Error_pG10Foundation10URLRequestVSg_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCAI0B0VSgtcF) `
    
    Validates the request, using the specified closure.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_validation_` | `[Validation](../Classes/DataRequest.html#/s:9Alamofire11DataRequestC10Validationa) ` closure used to validate the response. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The instance.
    
*   `[onHTTPResponse(on:perform:)](#/s:9Alamofire11DataRequestC14onHTTPResponse0D07performACXDSo17OS_dispatch_queueC_ySo17NSHTTPURLResponseC_yAA0C0C19ResponseDispositionOctctF) `
    
    Sets a closure called whenever the `DataRequest` produces an `HTTPURLResponse` and providing a completion handler to return a `ResponseDisposition` value.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_queue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which the closure will be called. `.main` by default. |
    | `_handler_` | Closure called when the instance produces an `HTTPURLResponse`. The `completionHandler` provided MUST be called, otherwise the request will never complete. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The instance.
    
*   `[onHTTPResponse(on:perform:)](#/s:9Alamofire11DataRequestC14onHTTPResponse0D07performACXDSo17OS_dispatch_queueC_ySo17NSHTTPURLResponseCctF) `

*   `[validate()](#/s:9Alamofire11DataRequestC8validateACXDyF) `
    
    Validates that the response has a status code in the default acceptable range of 200…299, and that the content type matches any specified in the Accept HTTP header field.
    
    If validation fails, subsequent calls to response handlers will have an associated error.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The request.

---

# DecodableResponseSerializer Class Reference

DecodableResponseSerializer
===========================

A `[ResponseSerializer](../Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` that decodes the response data as a `Decodable` value using any decoder that conforms to `[DataDecoder](../Protocols/DataDecoder.html) `. By default, this is an instance of `JSONDecoder`.

*   `[dataPreprocessor](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP16dataPreprocessorAA04DataE0_pvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[decoder](#/s:9Alamofire27DecodableResponseSerializerC7decoderAA11DataDecoder_pvp) `
    
    The `[DataDecoder](../Protocols/DataDecoder.html) ` instance used to decode responses.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[emptyResponseCodes](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP05emptyB5CodesShySiGvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[emptyRequestMethods](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP19emptyRequestMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(dataPreprocessor:decoder:emptyResponseCodes:emptyRequestMethods:)](#/s:9Alamofire27DecodableResponseSerializerC16dataPreprocessor7decoder05emptyC5Codes0H14RequestMethodsACyxGAA04DataF0_p_AA0L7Decoder_pShySiGShyAA10HTTPMethodVGtcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance using the values provided.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_dataPreprocessor_` | `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) ` used to prepare the received `Data` for serialization. |
    | `_decoder_` | The `[DataDecoder](../Protocols/DataDecoder.html) `. `JSONDecoder()` by default. |
    | `_emptyResponseCodes_` | The HTTP response codes for which empty responses are allowed. `[204, 205]` by default. |
    | `_emptyRequestMethods_` | The HTTP request methods for which empty responses are allowed. `[.head]` by default. |
    
*   `[serialize(request:response:data:error:)](#/s:9Alamofire30DataResponseSerializerProtocolP9serialize7request8response4data5error16SerializedObjectQz10Foundation10URLRequestVSg_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgAK0B0VSgs5Error_pSgtKF) `
    
    #### Declaration

# DefaultTrustEvaluator Class Reference

DefaultTrustEvaluator
=====================

An evaluator which uses the default server trust evaluation while allowing you to control whether to validate the host provided by the challenge. Applications are encouraged to always validate the host in production environments to guarantee the validity of the server’s certificate chain.

*   `[init(validateHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21DefaultTrustEvaluatorC12validateHostACSb_tcfc) `
    
    Creates a `DefaultTrustEvaluator`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_validateHost_` | Determines whether or not the evaluator should validate the host. `true` by default. |
    
*   `[evaluate(_:forHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingP8evaluate_7forHostySo03SecC3Refa_SStKF) `
    
    #### Declaration

---

# DisabledTrustEvaluator Class Reference

DisabledTrustEvaluator
======================

Disables all evaluation which in turn will always consider any server trust as valid.

**THIS EVALUATOR SHOULD NEVER BE USED IN PRODUCTION!**

*   `[init()](#/s:9Alamofire22DisabledTrustEvaluatorCACycfc) `
    
    Creates an instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[evaluate(_:forHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingP8evaluate_7forHostySo03SecC3Refa_SStKF) `
    
    #### Declaration

---

# Options Structure Reference

Options
=======

A set of options to be executed prior to moving a downloaded file from the temporary `URL` to the destination `URL`.

*   `[createIntermediateDirectories](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC7OptionsV29createIntermediateDirectoriesAEvpZ) `
    
    Specifies that intermediate directories for the destination URL should be created.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[removePreviousFile](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC7OptionsV18removePreviousFileAEvpZ) `
    
    Specifies that any previous file at the destination `URL` should be removed.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[rawValue](#/s:SY8rawValue03RawB0Qzvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(rawValue:)](#/s:s9OptionSetP8rawValuex03RawD0Qz_tcfc) `
    
    #### Declaration

# DownloadRequest Class Reference

DownloadRequest
===============

`[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` subclass which downloads `Data` to a file on disk using `URLSessionDownloadTask`.

*   `[Options](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC7OptionsV) `
    
    A set of options to be executed prior to moving a downloaded file from the temporary `URL` to the destination `URL`.
    
    [See more](../Classes/DownloadRequest/Options.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Destination)

### Destination

*   `[Destination](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC11Destinationa) `
    
    A closure executed once a `DownloadRequest` has successfully completed in order to determine where to move the temporary file written to during the download process. The closure takes two arguments: the temporary file URL and the `HTTPURLResponse`, and returns two values: the file URL where the temporary file should be moved and the options defining how the file should be moved.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[suggestedDownloadDestination(for:in:options:)](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC09suggestedB11Destination3for2in7options10Foundation3URLV011destinationJ0_AC7OptionsVAGtAJ_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCtYbcSo21NSSearchPathDirectoryV_So0nO10DomainMaskVAMtFZ) `
    
    Creates a download file destination closure which uses the default file manager to move the temporary file to a file URL in the first available directory with the specified search path directory and search path domain mask.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_directory_` | The search path directory. `.documentDirectory` by default. |
    | `_domain_` | The search path domain mask. `.userDomainMask` by default. |
    | `_options_` | `[DownloadRequest.Options](../Classes/DownloadRequest/Options.html) ` used when moving the downloaded file to its destination. None by default. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[Destination](../Classes/DownloadRequest.html#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC11Destinationa) ` closure.
    

[](#/Downloadable)

### Downloadable

*   `[Downloadable](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC12DownloadableO) `
    
    Type describing the source used to create the underlying `URLSessionDownloadTask`.
    
    [See more](../Classes/DownloadRequest/Downloadable.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Mutable%20State)

### Mutable State

*   `[resumeData](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC10resumeData10Foundation0E0VSgvp) `
    
    If the download is resumable and is eventually cancelled or fails, this value may be used to resume the download using the `download(resumingWith data:)` API.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[fileURL](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC7fileURL10Foundation0E0VSgvp) `

    #### Declaration

[](#/DownloadTask)

### DownloadTask

*   `[serializingData(automaticallyCancelling:dataPreprocessor:emptyResponseCodes:emptyRequestMethods:)](#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC15serializingData23automaticallyCancelling16dataPreprocessor18emptyResponseCodes0jC7MethodsAA0B4TaskVy10Foundation0E0VGSb_AA0eI0_pShySiGShyAA10HTTPMethodVGtF) `

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_shouldAutomaticallyCancel_` | `Bool` determining whether or not the request should be cancelled when the enclosing async context is cancelled. Only applies to `[DownloadTask](../Structs/DownloadTask.html) `‘s async properties. `true` by default. |
    | `_dataPreprocessor_` | `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) ` which processes the received `Data` before completion. |

# JSONResponseSerializer Class Reference

JSONResponseSerializer
======================

A `[ResponseSerializer](../Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` that decodes the response data using `JSONSerialization`. By default, a request returning `nil` or no data is considered an error. However, if the request has an `[HTTPMethod](../Structs/HTTPMethod.html) ` or the response has an HTTP status code valid for empty responses, then an `NSNull` value is returned.
