# MultipartFormData Class Reference

MultipartFormData
=================

Constructs `multipart/form-data` for uploads within an HTTP or HTTPS body. There are currently two ways to encode multipart form data. The first way is to encode the data directly in memory. This is very efficient, but can lead to memory issues if the dataset is too large. The second way is designed for larger datasets and will write all the data to a single file on disk with all the proper boundary segmentation. The second approach MUST be used for larger datasets such as video content, otherwise your app may run out of memory when trying to encode the dataset.

For more information on `multipart/form-data` in general, please refer to the RFC-2388 and RFC-2045 specs as well and the w3 form documentation.

*   [https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2388.txt](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2388.txt)
    
*   [https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2045.txt](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2045.txt)
    
*   [https://www.w3.org/TR/html401/interact/forms.html#h-17.13](https://www.w3.org/TR/html401/interact/forms.html#h-17.13)
    

[](#/Properties)

### Properties

*   `[encodingMemoryThreshold](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC23encodingMemoryThresholds6UInt64VvpZ) `
    
    Default memory threshold used when encoding `MultipartFormData`, in bytes.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[contentType](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC11contentTypeSSvp) `
    
    The `Content-Type` header value containing the boundary used to generate the `multipart/form-data`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[contentLength](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC13contentLengths6UInt64Vvp) `
    
    The content length of all body parts used to generate the `multipart/form-data` not including the boundaries.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[boundary](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC8boundarySSvp) `
    
    The boundary used to separate the body parts in the encoded form data.
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Lifecycle)

### Lifecycle

*   `[init(fileManager:boundary:)](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC11fileManager8boundaryACSo06NSFileF0C_SSSgtcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_fileManager_` | `FileManager` to use for file operations, if needed. |
    | `_boundary_` | Boundary `String` used to separate body parts. |
    

[](#/Body%20Parts)

### Body Parts

*   `[append(_:withName:fileName:mimeType:)](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC6append_8withName04fileG08mimeTypey10Foundation0D0V_S2SSgAKtF) `
    
    Creates a body part from the data and appends it to the instance.
    
    The body part data will be encoded using the following format:
    
    *   `Content-Disposition: form-data; name=#{name}; filename=#{filename}` (HTTP Header)
    *   `Content-Type: #{mimeType}` (HTTP Header)
    *   Encoded file data
    *   Multipart form boundary
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_data_` | `Data` to encoding into the instance. |
    | `_name_` | Name to associate with the `Data` in the `Content-Disposition` HTTP header. |
    | `_fileName_` | Filename to associate with the `Data` in the `Content-Disposition` HTTP header. |
    | `_mimeType_` | MIME type to associate with the data in the `Content-Type` HTTP header. |
    
*   `[append(_:withName:)](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC6append_8withNamey10Foundation3URLV_SStF) `
    
    Creates a body part from the file and appends it to the instance.
    
    The body part data will be encoded using the following format:
    
    *   `Content-Disposition: form-data; name=#{name}; filename=#{generated filename}` (HTTP Header)
    *   `Content-Type: #{generated mimeType}` (HTTP Header)
    *   Encoded file data
    *   Multipart form boundary
    
    The filename in the `Content-Disposition` HTTP header is generated from the last path component of the `fileURL`. The `Content-Type` HTTP header MIME type is generated by mapping the `fileURL` extension to the system associated MIME type.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_fileURL_` | `URL` of the file whose content will be encoded into the instance. |
    | `_name_` | Name to associate with the file content in the `Content-Disposition` HTTP header. |
    
*   `[append(_:withName:fileName:mimeType:)](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC6append_8withName04fileG08mimeTypey10Foundation3URLV_S3StF) `
    
    Creates a body part from the file and appends it to the instance.
    
    The body part data will be encoded using the following format:
    
    *   Content-Disposition: form-data; name=#{name}; filename=#{filename} (HTTP Header)
    *   Content-Type: #{mimeType} (HTTP Header)
    *   Encoded file data
    *   Multipart form boundary
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_fileURL_` | `URL` of the file whose content will be encoded into the instance. |
    | `_name_` | Name to associate with the file content in the `Content-Disposition` HTTP header. |
    | `_fileName_` | Filename to associate with the file content in the `Content-Disposition` HTTP header. |
    | `_mimeType_` | MIME type to associate with the file content in the `Content-Type` HTTP header. |
    
*   `[append(_:withLength:name:fileName:mimeType:)](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC6append_10withLength4name8fileName8mimeTypeySo13NSInputStreamC_s6UInt64VS3StF) `
    
    Creates a body part from the stream and appends it to the instance.
    
    The body part data will be encoded using the following format:
    
    *   `Content-Disposition: form-data; name=#{name}; filename=#{filename}` (HTTP Header)
    *   `Content-Type: #{mimeType}` (HTTP Header)
    *   Encoded stream data
    *   Multipart form boundary
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_stream_` | `InputStream` to encode into the instance. |
    | `_length_` | Length, in bytes, of the stream. |
    | `_name_` | Name to associate with the stream content in the `Content-Disposition` HTTP header. |
    | `_fileName_` | Filename to associate with the stream content in the `Content-Disposition` HTTP header. |
    | `_mimeType_` | MIME type to associate with the stream content in the `Content-Type` HTTP header. |
    
*   `[append(_:withLength:headers:)](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC6append_10withLength7headersySo13NSInputStreamC_s6UInt64VAA11HTTPHeadersVtF) `
    
    Creates a body part with the stream, length, and headers and appends it to the instance.
    
    The body part data will be encoded using the following format:
    
    *   HTTP headers
    *   Encoded stream data
    *   Multipart form boundary
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_stream_` | `InputStream` to encode into the instance. |
    | `_length_` | Length, in bytes, of the stream. |
    | `_headers_` | `[HTTPHeaders](../Structs/HTTPHeaders.html) ` for the body part. |
    

[](#/Data%20Encoding)

### Data Encoding

*   `[encode()](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC6encode10Foundation0D0VyKF) `

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Return Value

*   `[writeEncodedData(to:)](#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC012writeEncodedD02toy10Foundation3URLV_tKF) `
    
    Writes all appended body parts to the given file `URL`.
    
    This process is facilitated by reading and writing with input and output streams, respectively. Thus, this approach is very memory efficient and should be used for large body part data.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_fileURL_` | File `URL` to which to write the form data. |

# PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator Class Reference

PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator
================================

Uses the pinned certificates to validate the server trust. The server trust is considered valid if one of the pinned certificates match one of the server certificates. By validating both the certificate chain and host, certificate pinning provides a very secure form of server trust validation mitigating most, if not all, MITM attacks. Applications are encouraged to always validate the host and require a valid certificate chain in production environments.

*   `[init(certificates:acceptSelfSignedCertificates:performDefaultValidation:validateHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire32PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluatorC12certificates016acceptSelfSignedC024performDefaultValidation12validateHostACSaySo17SecCertificateRefaG_S3btcfc) `
    
    Creates a `PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator` from the provided parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_certificates_` | The certificates to use to evaluate the trust. All `cer`, `crt`, and `der` certificates in `Bundle.main` by default. |
    | `_acceptSelfSignedCertificates_` | Adds the provided certificates as anchors for the trust evaluation, allowing self-signed certificates to pass. `false` by default. THIS SETTING SHOULD BE FALSE IN PRODUCTION! |
    | `_performDefaultValidation_` | Determines whether default validation should be performed in addition to evaluating the pinned certificates. `true` by default. |
    | `_validateHost_` | Determines whether or not the evaluator should validate the host, in addition to performing the default evaluation, even if `performDefaultValidation` is `false`. `true` by default. |
    
*   `[evaluate(_:forHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingP8evaluate_7forHostySo03SecC3Refa_SStKF) `
    
    #### Declaration

---

# NetworkReachabilityManager Class Reference

NetworkReachabilityManager
==========================

The `NetworkReachabilityManager` class listens for reachability changes of hosts and addresses for both cellular and WiFi network interfaces.

Reachability can be used to determine background information about why a network operation failed, or to retry network requests when a connection is established. It should not be used to prevent a user from initiating a network request, as it’s possible that an initial request may be required to establish reachability.

*   `[NetworkReachabilityStatus](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC0bC6StatusO) `
    
    Defines the various states of network reachability.
    
    [See more](../Classes/NetworkReachabilityManager/NetworkReachabilityStatus.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Listener](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC8Listenera) `
    
    A closure executed when the network reachability status changes. The closure takes a single argument: the network reachability status.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[default](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC7defaultACSgvpZ) `
    
    Default `NetworkReachabilityManager` for the zero address and a `listenerQueue` of `.main`.
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Properties)

### Properties

*   `[isReachable](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC11isReachableSbvp) `
    
    Whether the network is currently reachable.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[isReachableOnCellular](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC21isReachableOnCellularSbvp) `
    
    Whether the network is currently reachable over the cellular interface.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[isReachableOnEthernetOrWiFi](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC27isReachableOnEthernetOrWiFiSbvp) `
    
    Whether the network is currently reachable over Ethernet or WiFi interface.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[reachabilityQueue](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC17reachabilityQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) `
    
    `DispatchQueue` on which reachability will update.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[flags](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerC5flagsSo09SCNetworkC5FlagsVSgvp) `
    
    Flags of the current reachability type, if any.
    
    #### Declaration

    The current network reachability status.
    
    #### Declaration

    Creates an instance with the specified host.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_host_` | Host used to evaluate network reachability. Must _not_ include the scheme (e.g. `https`). |
    
*   `[init()](#/s:9Alamofire26NetworkReachabilityManagerCACSgycfc) `
    
    Creates an instance that monitors the address 0.0.0.0.
    
    Reachability treats the 0.0.0.0 address as a special token that causes it to monitor the general routing status of the device, both IPv4 and IPv6.
    
    #### Declaration

# PublicKeysTrustEvaluator Class Reference

PublicKeysTrustEvaluator
========================

Uses the pinned public keys to validate the server trust. The server trust is considered valid if one of the pinned public keys match one of the server certificate public keys. By validating both the certificate chain and host, public key pinning provides a very secure form of server trust validation mitigating most, if not all, MITM attacks. Applications are encouraged to always validate the host and require a valid certificate chain in production environments.

*   `[init(keys:performDefaultValidation:validateHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire24PublicKeysTrustEvaluatorC4keys24performDefaultValidation12validateHostACSaySo9SecKeyRefaG_S2btcfc) `
    
    Creates a `PublicKeysTrustEvaluator` from the provided parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_keys_` | The `SecKey`s to use to validate public keys. Defaults to the public keys of all certificates included in the main bundle. |
    | `_performDefaultValidation_` | Determines whether default validation should be performed in addition to evaluating the pinned certificates. `true` by default. |
    | `_validateHost_` | Determines whether or not the evaluator should validate the host, in addition to performing the default evaluation, even if `performDefaultValidation` is `false`. `true` by default. |
    
*   `[evaluate(_:forHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingP8evaluate_7forHostySo03SecC3Refa_SStKF) `
    
    #### Declaration

---

# RetryPolicy Class Reference

RetryPolicy
===========

A retry policy that retries requests using an exponential backoff for allowed HTTP methods and HTTP status codes as well as certain types of networking errors.

*   `[defaultRetryLimit](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC07defaultB5LimitSuvpZ) `
    
    The default retry limit for retry policies.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultExponentialBackoffBase](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC29defaultExponentialBackoffBaseSuvpZ) `
    
    The default exponential backoff base for retry policies (must be a minimum of 2).
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultExponentialBackoffScale](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC30defaultExponentialBackoffScaleSdvpZ) `
    
    The default exponential backoff scale for retry policies.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultRetryableHTTPMethods](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC27defaultRetryableHTTPMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvpZ) `
    
    The default HTTP methods to retry. See [RFC 2616 - Section 9.1.2](https://www.w3.org/Protocols/rfc2616/rfc2616-sec9.html)
     for more information.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultRetryableHTTPStatusCodes](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC31defaultRetryableHTTPStatusCodesShySiGvpZ) `
    
    The default HTTP status codes to retry. See [RFC 2616 - Section 10](https://www.w3.org/Protocols/rfc2616/rfc2616-sec10.html#sec10)
     for more information.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultRetryableURLErrorCodes](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC29defaultRetryableURLErrorCodesShy10Foundation0F0V4CodeVGvpZ) `
    
    The default URL error codes to retry.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[retryLimit](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC10retryLimitSuvp) `
    
    The total number of times the request is allowed to be retried.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[exponentialBackoffBase](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC22exponentialBackoffBaseSuvp) `
    
    The base of the exponential backoff policy (should always be greater than or equal to 2).
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[exponentialBackoffScale](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC23exponentialBackoffScaleSdvp) `
    
    The scale of the exponential backoff.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[retryableHTTPMethods](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC20retryableHTTPMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvp) `
    
    The HTTP methods that are allowed to be retried.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[retryableHTTPStatusCodes](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC24retryableHTTPStatusCodesShySiGvp) `
    
    The HTTP status codes that are automatically retried by the policy.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[retryableURLErrorCodes](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC22retryableURLErrorCodesShy10Foundation0E0V4CodeVGvp) `
    
    The URL error codes that are automatically retried by the policy.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(retryLimit:exponentialBackoffBase:exponentialBackoffScale:retryableHTTPMethods:retryableHTTPStatusCodes:retryableURLErrorCodes:)](#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC10retryLimit22exponentialBackoffBase0fG5Scale20retryableHTTPMethods0J15HTTPStatusCodes0j8URLErrorM0ACSu_SuSdShyAA10HTTPMethodVGShySiGShy10Foundation0N0V4CodeVGtcfc) `
    
    Creates a `RetryPolicy` from the specified parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_retryLimit_` | The total number of times the request is allowed to be retried. `2` by default. |
    | `_exponentialBackoffBase_` | The base of the exponential backoff policy. `2` by default. |
    | `_exponentialBackoffScale_` | The scale of the exponential backoff. `0.5` by default. |
    | `_retryableHTTPMethods_` | The HTTP methods that are allowed to be retried. `[RetryPolicy.defaultRetryableHTTPMethods](../Classes/RetryPolicy.html#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC27defaultRetryableHTTPMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvpZ) ` by default. |
    | `_retryableHTTPStatusCodes_` | The HTTP status codes that are automatically retried by the policy. `[RetryPolicy.defaultRetryableHTTPStatusCodes](../Classes/RetryPolicy.html#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC31defaultRetryableHTTPStatusCodesShySiGvpZ) ` by default. |
    | `_retryableURLErrorCodes_` | The URL error codes that are automatically retried by the policy. `[RetryPolicy.defaultRetryableURLErrorCodes](../Classes/RetryPolicy.html#/s:9Alamofire11RetryPolicyC29defaultRetryableURLErrorCodesShy10Foundation0F0V4CodeVGvpZ) ` by default. |
    
*   `[retry(_:for:dueTo:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestRetrierP5retry_3for5dueTo10completionyAA0B0C_AA7SessionCs5Error_pyAA11RetryResultOYbctF) `
    
    #### Declaration

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` that failed due to the provided `Error`. |
    | `_error_` | `Error` encountered while executing the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    `Bool` determining whether or not to retry the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `.

# RevocationTrustEvaluator Class Reference

RevocationTrustEvaluator
========================

An evaluator which Uses the default and revoked server trust evaluations allowing you to control whether to validate the host provided by the challenge as well as specify the revocation flags for testing for revoked certificates. Apple platforms did not start testing for revoked certificates automatically until iOS 10.1, macOS 10.12 and tvOS 10.1 which is demonstrated in our TLS tests. Applications are encouraged to always validate the host in production environments to guarantee the validity of the server’s certificate chain.

*   `[Options](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV) `
    
    Represents the options to be use when evaluating the status of a certificate. Only Revocation Policy Constants are valid, and can be found in [Apple’s documentation](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/security/certificate_key_and_trust_services/policies/1563600-revocation_policy_constants)
    .
    
    [See more](../Classes/RevocationTrustEvaluator/Options.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(performDefaultValidation:validateHost:options:)](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC24performDefaultValidation12validateHost7optionsACSb_SbAC7OptionsVtcfc) `
    
    Creates a `RevocationTrustEvaluator` using the provided parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_performDefaultValidation_` | Determines whether default validation should be performed in addition to evaluating the pinned certificates. `true` by default. |
    | `_validateHost_` | Determines whether or not the evaluator should validate the host, in addition to performing the default evaluation, even if `performDefaultValidation` is `false`. `true` by default. |
    | `_options_` | The `[Options](../Classes/RevocationTrustEvaluator/Options.html) ` to use to check the revocation status of the certificate. `.any` by default. |
    
*   `[evaluate(_:forHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingP8evaluate_7forHostySo03SecC3Refa_SStKF) `
    
    #### Declaration

---

# Options Structure Reference

Options
=======

Represents the options to be use when evaluating the status of a certificate. Only Revocation Policy Constants are valid, and can be found in [Apple’s documentation](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/security/certificate_key_and_trust_services/policies/1563600-revocation_policy_constants)
.

*   `[crl](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV3crlAEvpZ) `
    
    Perform revocation checking using the CRL (Certification Revocation List) method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[networkAccessDisabled](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV21networkAccessDisabledAEvpZ) `
    
    Consult only locally cached replies; do not use network access.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ocsp](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV4ocspAEvpZ) `
    
    Perform revocation checking using OCSP (Online Certificate Status Protocol).
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[preferCRL](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV9preferCRLAEvpZ) `
    
    Prefer CRL revocation checking over OCSP; by default, OCSP is preferred.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[requirePositiveResponse](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV23requirePositiveResponseAEvpZ) `
    
    Require a positive response to pass the policy. If the flag is not set, revocation checking is done on a “best attempt” basis, where failure to reach the server is not considered fatal.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[any](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV3anyAEvpZ) `
    
    Perform either OCSP or CRL checking. The checking is performed according to the method(s) specified in the certificate and the value of `[preferCRL](../../Classes/RevocationTrustEvaluator/Options.html#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV9preferCRLAEvpZ) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[rawValue](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV8rawValueSuvp) `
    
    The raw value of the option.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(rawValue:)](#/s:9Alamofire24RevocationTrustEvaluatorC7OptionsV8rawValueAESu_tcfc) `
    
    Creates an `Options` value with the given `CFOptionFlags`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_rawValue_` | The `CFOptionFlags` value to initialize with. |

---

# ServerTrustManager Class Reference

ServerTrustManager
==================

Responsible for managing the mapping of `[ServerTrustEvaluating](../Protocols/ServerTrustEvaluating.html) ` values to given hosts.

*   `[allHostsMustBeEvaluated](#/s:9Alamofire18ServerTrustManagerC23allHostsMustBeEvaluatedSbvp) `
    
    Determines whether all hosts for this `ServerTrustManager` must be evaluated. `true` by default.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[evaluators](#/s:9Alamofire18ServerTrustManagerC10evaluatorsSDySSAA0bC10Evaluating_pGvp) `
    
    The dictionary of policies mapped to a particular host.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(allHostsMustBeEvaluated:evaluators:)](#/s:9Alamofire18ServerTrustManagerC23allHostsMustBeEvaluated10evaluatorsACSb_SDySSAA0bC10Evaluating_pGtcfc) `
    
    Initializes the `ServerTrustManager` instance with the given evaluators.
    
    Since different servers and web services can have different leaf certificates, intermediate and even root certificates, it is important to have the flexibility to specify evaluation policies on a per host basis. This allows for scenarios such as using default evaluation for host1, certificate pinning for host2, public key pinning for host3 and disabling evaluation for host4.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_allHostsMustBeEvaluated_` | The value determining whether all hosts for this instance must be evaluated. `true` by default. |
    | `_evaluators_` | A dictionary of evaluators mapped to hosts. |
    
*   `[serverTrustEvaluator(forHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire18ServerTrustManagerC06serverC9Evaluator7forHostAA0bC10Evaluating_pSgSS_tKF) `
    
    Returns the `[ServerTrustEvaluating](../Protocols/ServerTrustEvaluating.html) ` value for the given host, if one is set.
    
    By default, this method will return the policy that perfectly matches the given host. Subclasses could override this method and implement more complex mapping implementations such as wildcards.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_host_` | The host to use when searching for a matching policy. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[ServerTrustEvaluating](../Protocols/ServerTrustEvaluating.html) ` value for the given host if found, `nil` otherwise.

---

# Request Class Reference

Request
=======

`Request` is the common superclass of all Alamofire request types and provides common state, delegate, and callback handling.

*   `[State](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC5StateO) `
    
    State of the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `, with managed transitions between states set when calling `[resume()](../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6resumeACXDyF) `, `[suspend()](../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC7suspendACXDyF) `, or `[cancel()](../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6cancelACXDyF) ` on the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `.
    
    [See more](../Classes/Request/State.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Initial%20State)

### Initial State

*   `[id](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC2id10Foundation4UUIDVvp) `
    
    `UUID` providing a unique identifier for the `Request`, used in the `Hashable` and `Equatable` conformances.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[underlyingQueue](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC15underlyingQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) `
    
    The serial queue for all internal async actions.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[serializationQueue](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC18serializationQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) `
    
    The queue used for all serialization actions. By default it’s a serial queue that targets `[underlyingQueue](../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC15underlyingQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[eventMonitor](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC12eventMonitorAA05EventD0_pSgvp) `
    
    `[EventMonitor](../Protocols/EventMonitor.html) ` used for event callbacks.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[interceptor](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC11interceptorAA0B11Interceptor_pSgvp) `
    
    The `Request`‘s interceptor.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[delegate](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC8delegateAA0B8Delegate_pSgvp) `
    
    The `Request`‘s delegate.
    
    #### Declaration

### Mutable State

# State Enumeration Reference

State
=====

State of the `[Request](../../Classes/Request.html) `, with managed transitions between states set when calling `[resume()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6resumeACXDyF) `, `[suspend()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC7suspendACXDyF) `, or `[cancel()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6cancelACXDyF) ` on the `[Request](../../Classes/Request.html) `.

*   `[initialized](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC5StateO11initializedyA2EmF) `
    
    Initial state of the `[Request](../../Classes/Request.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[resumed](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC5StateO7resumedyA2EmF) `
    
    `State` set when `[resume()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6resumeACXDyF) ` is called. Any tasks created for the `[Request](../../Classes/Request.html) ` will have `[resume()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6resumeACXDyF) ` called on them in this state.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[suspended](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC5StateO9suspendedyA2EmF) `
    
    `State` set when `[suspend()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC7suspendACXDyF) ` is called. Any tasks created for the `[Request](../../Classes/Request.html) ` will have `[suspend()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC7suspendACXDyF) ` called on them in this state.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[cancelled](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC5StateO9cancelledyA2EmF) `
    
    `State` set when `[cancel()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6cancelACXDyF) ` is called. Any tasks created for the `[Request](../../Classes/Request.html) ` will have `[cancel()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6cancelACXDyF) ` called on them. Unlike `[resumed](../../Classes/Request/State.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC5StateO7resumedyA2EmF) ` or `[suspended](../../Classes/Request/State.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC5StateO9suspendedyA2EmF) `, once in the `cancelled` state, the `[Request](../../Classes/Request.html) ` can no longer transition to any other state.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[finished](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC5StateO8finishedyA2EmF) `
    
    `State` set when all response serialization completion closures have been cleared on the `[Request](../../Classes/Request.html) ` and enqueued on their respective queues.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# ResponseDisposition Enumeration Reference

ResponseDisposition
===================

Type indicating how a `[DataRequest](../../Classes/DataRequest.html) ` or `[DataStreamRequest](../../Classes/DataStreamRequest.html) ` should proceed after receiving an `HTTPURLResponse`.

*   `[allow](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC19ResponseDispositionO5allowyA2EmF) `
    
    Allow the request to continue normally.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[cancel](#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC19ResponseDispositionO6cancelyA2EmF) `
    
    Cancel the request, similar to calling `[cancel()](../../Classes/Request.html#/s:9Alamofire7RequestC6cancelACXDyF) `.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# StringResponseSerializer Class Reference

StringResponseSerializer
========================

A `[ResponseSerializer](../Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` that decodes the response data as a `String`. By default, a request returning `nil` or no data is considered an error. However, if the request has an `[HTTPMethod](../Structs/HTTPMethod.html) ` or the response has an HTTP status code valid for empty responses, then an empty `String` is returned.

*   `[dataPreprocessor](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP16dataPreprocessorAA04DataE0_pvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[encoding](#/s:9Alamofire24StringResponseSerializerC8encodingSS10FoundationE8EncodingVSgvp) `
    
    Optional string encoding used to validate the response.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[emptyResponseCodes](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP05emptyB5CodesShySiGvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[emptyRequestMethods](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP19emptyRequestMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(dataPreprocessor:encoding:emptyResponseCodes:emptyRequestMethods:)](#/s:9Alamofire24StringResponseSerializerC16dataPreprocessor8encoding05emptyC5Codes0H14RequestMethodsAcA04DataF0_p_SS10FoundationE8EncodingVSgShySiGShyAA10HTTPMethodVGtcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance with the provided values.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_dataPreprocessor_` | `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) ` used to prepare the received `Data` for serialization. |
    | `_encoding_` | A string encoding. Defaults to `nil`, in which case the encoding will be determined from the server response, falling back to the default HTTP character set, `ISO-8859-1`. |
    | `_emptyResponseCodes_` | The HTTP response codes for which empty responses are allowed. `[204, 205]` by default. |
    | `_emptyRequestMethods_` | The HTTP request methods for which empty responses are allowed. `[.head]` by default. |
    
*   `[serialize(request:response:data:error:)](#/s:9Alamofire30DataResponseSerializerProtocolP9serialize7request8response4data5error16SerializedObjectQz10Foundation10URLRequestVSg_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgAK0B0VSgs5Error_pSgtKF) `
    
    #### Declaration

---

# Session Class Reference

Session
=======

`Session` creates and manages Alamofire’s `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` types during their lifetimes. It also provides common functionality for all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s, including queuing, interception, trust management, redirect handling, and response cache handling.

*   `[default](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC7defaultACvpZ) `
    
    Shared singleton instance used by all `AF.request` APIs. Cannot be modified.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[session](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC7sessionSo12NSURLSessionCvp) `
    
    Underlying `URLSession` used to create `URLSessionTasks` for this instance, and for which this instance’s `[delegate](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC8delegateAA0B8DelegateCvp) ` handles `URLSessionDelegate` callbacks.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[delegate](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC8delegateAA0B8DelegateCvp) `
    
    Instance’s `[SessionDelegate](../Classes/SessionDelegate.html) `, which handles the `URLSessionDelegate` methods and `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` interaction.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[rootQueue](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC9rootQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) `
    
    Root `DispatchQueue` for all internal callbacks and state update. **MUST** be a serial queue.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[startRequestsImmediately](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC24startRequestsImmediatelySbvp) `
    
    Value determining whether this instance automatically calls `resume()` on all created `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[requestQueue](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC12requestQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) `
    
    `DispatchQueue` on which `URLRequest`s are created asynchronously. By default this queue uses `[rootQueue](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC9rootQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) ` as its `target`, but a separate queue can be used if request creation is determined to be a bottleneck. Always profile and test before introducing an additional queue.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[serializationQueue](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC18serializationQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) `
    
    `DispatchQueue` passed to all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s on which they perform their response serialization. By default this queue uses `[rootQueue](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC9rootQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) ` as its `target` but a separate queue can be used if response serialization is determined to be a bottleneck. Always profile and test before introducing an additional queue.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[interceptor](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC11interceptorAA18RequestInterceptor_pSgvp) `
    
    `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) ` used for all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` created by the instance. `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) `s can also be set on a per-`[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` basis, in which case the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `‘s interceptor takes precedence over this value.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[serverTrustManager](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC18serverTrustManagerAA06ServerdE0CSgvp) `
    
    `[ServerTrustManager](../Classes/ServerTrustManager.html) ` instance used to evaluate all trust challenges and provide certificate and key pinning.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[redirectHandler](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC15redirectHandlerAA08RedirectD0_pSgvp) `
    
    `[RedirectHandler](../Protocols/RedirectHandler.html) ` instance used to provide customization for request redirection.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[cachedResponseHandler](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC21cachedResponseHandlerAA06CacheddE0_pSgvp) `
    
    `[CachedResponseHandler](../Protocols/CachedResponseHandler.html) ` instance used to provide customization of cached response handling.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[eventMonitor](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC12eventMonitorAA014CompositeEventD0Cvp) `
    
    `[CompositeEventMonitor](../Classes/CompositeEventMonitor.html) ` used to compose any passed `[EventMonitor](../Protocols/EventMonitor.html) `s.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultEventMonitors](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC20defaultEventMonitorsSayAA0D7Monitor_pGvp) `
    
    `[EventMonitor](../Protocols/EventMonitor.html) `s included in all instances unless overwritten. `[AlamofireNotifications()]` by default.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(session:delegate:rootQueue:startRequestsImmediately:requestQueue:serializationQueue:interceptor:serverTrustManager:redirectHandler:cachedResponseHandler:eventMonitors:)](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC7session8delegate9rootQueue24startRequestsImmediately07requestF0013serializationF011interceptor18serverTrustManager15redirectHandler014cachedResponseQ013eventMonitorsACSo12NSURLSessionC_AA0B8DelegateCSo17OS_dispatch_queueCSbATSgAuA18RequestInterceptor_pSgAA06ServernO0CSgAA08RedirectQ0_pSgAA06CachedsQ0_pSgSayAA12EventMonitor_pGtcfc) `
    
    Creates a `Session` from a `URLSession` and other parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_session_` | Underlying `URLSession` for this instance. |
    | `_delegate_` | `[SessionDelegate](../Classes/SessionDelegate.html) ` that handles `[session](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC7sessionSo12NSURLSessionCvp) `‘s delegate callbacks as well as `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` interaction. |
    | `_rootQueue_` | Root `DispatchQueue` for all internal callbacks and state updates. **MUST** be a serial queue. |
    | `_startRequestsImmediately_` | Determines whether this instance will automatically start all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s. `true` by default. If set to `false`, all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s created must have `.resume()` called. on them for them to start. |
    | `_requestQueue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which to perform `URLRequest` creation. By default this queue will use the `[rootQueue](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC9rootQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) ` as its `target`. A separate queue can be used if it’s determined request creation is a bottleneck, but that should only be done after careful testing and profiling. `nil` by default. |
    | `_serializationQueue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which to perform all response serialization. By default this queue will use the `[rootQueue](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC9rootQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) ` as its `target`. A separate queue can be used if it’s determined response serialization is a bottleneck, but that should only be done after careful testing and profiling. `nil` by default. |
    | `_interceptor_` | `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) ` to be used for all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s created by this instance. `nil` by default. |
    | `_serverTrustManager_` | `[ServerTrustManager](../Classes/ServerTrustManager.html) ` to be used for all trust evaluations by this instance. `nil` by default. |
    | `_redirectHandler_` | `[RedirectHandler](../Protocols/RedirectHandler.html) ` to be used by all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s created by this instance. `nil` by default. |
    | `_cachedResponseHandler_` | `[CachedResponseHandler](../Protocols/CachedResponseHandler.html) ` to be used by all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s created by this instance. `nil` by default. |
    | `_eventMonitors_` | `[EventMonitor](../Protocols/EventMonitor.html) `s used by the instance. `[AlamofireNotifications()]` by default. |
    
*   `[init(configuration:delegate:rootQueue:startRequestsImmediately:requestQueue:serializationQueue:interceptor:serverTrustManager:redirectHandler:cachedResponseHandler:eventMonitors:)](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC13configuration8delegate9rootQueue24startRequestsImmediately07requestF0013serializationF011interceptor18serverTrustManager15redirectHandler014cachedResponseQ013eventMonitorsACSo25NSURLSessionConfigurationC_AA0B8DelegateCSo17OS_dispatch_queueCSbATSgAuA18RequestInterceptor_pSgAA06ServernO0CSgAA08RedirectQ0_pSgAA06CachedsQ0_pSgSayAA12EventMonitor_pGtcfc) `
    
    Creates a `Session` from a `URLSessionConfiguration`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_configuration_` | `URLSessionConfiguration` to be used to create the underlying `URLSession`. Changes to this value after being passed to this initializer will have no effect. `URLSessionConfiguration.af.default` by default. |
    | `_delegate_` | `[SessionDelegate](../Classes/SessionDelegate.html) ` that handles `[session](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC7sessionSo12NSURLSessionCvp) `‘s delegate callbacks as well as `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` interaction. `SessionDelegate()` by default. |
    | `_rootQueue_` | Root `DispatchQueue` for all internal callbacks and state updates. **MUST** be a serial queue. `DispatchQueue(label: "org.alamofire.session.rootQueue")` by default. |
    | `_startRequestsImmediately_` | Determines whether this instance will automatically start all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s. `true` by default. If set to `false`, all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s created must have `.resume()` called. on them for them to start. |
    | `_requestQueue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which to perform `URLRequest` creation. By default this queue will use the `[rootQueue](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC9rootQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) ` as its `target`. A separate queue can be used if it’s determined request creation is a bottleneck, but that should only be done after careful testing and profiling. `nil` by default. |
    | `_serializationQueue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which to perform all response serialization. By default this queue will use the `[rootQueue](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC9rootQueueSo17OS_dispatch_queueCvp) ` as its `target`. A separate queue can be used if it’s determined response serialization is a bottleneck, but that should only be done after careful testing and profiling. `nil` by default. |
    | `_interceptor_` | `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) ` to be used for all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s created by this instance. `nil` by default. |
    | `_serverTrustManager_` | `[ServerTrustManager](../Classes/ServerTrustManager.html) ` to be used for all trust evaluations by this instance. `nil` by default. |
    | `_redirectHandler_` | `[RedirectHandler](../Protocols/RedirectHandler.html) ` to be used by all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s created by this instance. `nil` by default. |
    | `_cachedResponseHandler_` | `[CachedResponseHandler](../Protocols/CachedResponseHandler.html) ` to be used by all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s created by this instance. `nil` by default. |
    | `_eventMonitors_` | `[EventMonitor](../Protocols/EventMonitor.html) `s used by the instance. `[AlamofireNotifications()]` by default. |

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_queue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which the completion handler is run. `.main` by default. |
    | `_completion_` | Closure to be called when all `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `s have been cancelled. |

### DownloadRequest

    | `_convertible_` | `[URLConvertible](../Protocols/URLConvertible.html) ` value to be used as the `URLRequest`‘s `URL`. |
    | `_method_` | `[HTTPMethod](../Structs/HTTPMethod.html) ` for the `URLRequest`. `.get` by default. |
    | `_parameters_` | Value conforming to `Encodable` to be encoded into the `URLRequest`. `nil` by default. |
    | `_encoder_` | `[ParameterEncoder](../Protocols/ParameterEncoder.html) ` to be used to encode the `parameters` value into the `URLRequest`. Defaults to `[URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder.default](../Classes/URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder.html#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC7defaultACvpZ) `. |
    | `_headers_` | `[HTTPHeaders](../Structs/HTTPHeaders.html) ` value to be added to the `URLRequest`. `nil` by default. |
    | `_interceptor_` | `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) ` value to be used by the returned `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) `. `nil` by default. |
    | `_requestModifier_` | `[RequestModifier](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC15RequestModifiera) ` which will be applied to the `URLRequest` created from the provided parameters. `nil` by default. |
    | `_destination_` | `[DownloadRequest.Destination](../Classes/DownloadRequest.html#/s:9Alamofire15DownloadRequestC11Destinationa) ` closure used to determine how and where the downloaded file should be moved. `nil` by default. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The created `[DownloadRequest](../Classes/DownloadRequest.html) `.

[](#/MultipartFormData)

### MultipartFormData

*   `[upload(multipartFormData:to:usingThreshold:method:headers:interceptor:fileManager:requestModifier:)](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC6upload17multipartFormData2to14usingThreshold6method7headers11interceptor11fileManager15requestModifierAA13UploadRequestCyAA09MultiparteF0Cc_AA14URLConvertible_ps6UInt64VAA10HTTPMethodVAA11HTTPHeadersVSgAA0R11Interceptor_pSgSo06NSFileN0Cy10Foundation10URLRequestVzYbKcSgtF) `
    
    Creates an `[UploadRequest](../Classes/UploadRequest.html) ` for the multipart form data built using a closure and sent using the provided `URLRequest` components and `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) `.
    
    It is important to understand the memory implications of uploading `[MultipartFormData](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html) `. If the cumulative payload is small, encoding the data in-memory and directly uploading to a server is the by far the most efficient approach. However, if the payload is too large, encoding the data in-memory could cause your app to be terminated. Larger payloads must first be written to disk using input and output streams to keep the memory footprint low, then the data can be uploaded as a stream from the resulting file. Streaming from disk MUST be used for larger payloads such as video content.
    
    The `encodingMemoryThreshold` parameter allows Alamofire to automatically determine whether to encode in-memory or stream from disk. If the content length of the `[MultipartFormData](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html) ` is below the `encodingMemoryThreshold`, encoding takes place in-memory. If the content length exceeds the threshold, the data is streamed to disk during the encoding process. Then the result is uploaded as data or as a stream depending on which encoding technique was used.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_multipartFormData_` | `[MultipartFormData](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html) ` building closure. |
    | `_url_` | `[URLConvertible](../Protocols/URLConvertible.html) ` value to be used as the `URLRequest`‘s `URL`. |
    | `_encodingMemoryThreshold_` | Byte threshold used to determine whether the form data is encoded into memory or onto disk before being uploaded. `[MultipartFormData.encodingMemoryThreshold](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC23encodingMemoryThresholds6UInt64VvpZ) ` by default. |
    | `_method_` | `[HTTPMethod](../Structs/HTTPMethod.html) ` for the `URLRequest`. `.post` by default. |
    | `_headers_` | `[HTTPHeaders](../Structs/HTTPHeaders.html) ` value to be added to the `URLRequest`. `nil` by default. |
    | `_interceptor_` | `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) ` value to be used by the returned `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) `. `nil` by default. |
    | `_fileManager_` | `FileManager` to be used if the form data exceeds the memory threshold and is written to disk before being uploaded. `[.default](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC7defaultACvpZ) ` instance by default. |
    | `_requestModifier_` | `[RequestModifier](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC15RequestModifiera) ` which will be applied to the `URLRequest` created from the provided parameters. `nil` by default. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The created `[UploadRequest](../Classes/UploadRequest.html) `.
    
*   `[upload(multipartFormData:with:usingThreshold:interceptor:fileManager:)](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC6upload17multipartFormData4with14usingThreshold11interceptor11fileManagerAA13UploadRequestCyAA09MultiparteF0Cc_AA21URLRequestConvertible_ps6UInt64VAA0N11Interceptor_pSgSo06NSFileL0CtF) `
    
    Creates an `[UploadRequest](../Classes/UploadRequest.html) ` using a `[MultipartFormData](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html) ` building closure, the provided `[URLRequestConvertible](../Protocols/URLRequestConvertible.html) ` value, and a `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) `.
    
    It is important to understand the memory implications of uploading `[MultipartFormData](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html) `.     #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_multipartFormData_` | `[MultipartFormData](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html) ` building closure. |

    | `_encodingMemoryThreshold_` | Byte threshold used to determine whether the form data is encoded into memory or onto disk before being uploaded. `[MultipartFormData.encodingMemoryThreshold](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html#/s:9Alamofire17MultipartFormDataC23encodingMemoryThresholds6UInt64VvpZ) ` by default. |
    | `_interceptor_` | `[RequestInterceptor](../Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html) ` value to be used by the returned `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) `. `nil` by default. |
    | `_fileManager_` | `FileManager` to be used if the form data exceeds the memory threshold and is written to disk before being uploaded. `[.default](../Classes/Session.html#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC7defaultACvpZ) ` instance by default. |
    
    #### Return Value

*   `[upload(multipartFormData:to:usingThreshold:method:headers:interceptor:fileManager:requestModifier:)](#/s:9Alamofire7SessionC6upload17multipartFormData2to14usingThreshold6method7headers11interceptor11fileManager15requestModifierAA13UploadRequestCAA09MultiparteF0C_AA14URLConvertible_ps6UInt64VAA10HTTPMethodVAA11HTTPHeadersVSgAA0R11Interceptor_pSgSo06NSFileN0Cy10Foundation10URLRequestVzYbKcSgtF) `

# BoolEncoding Enumeration Reference

BoolEncoding
============

Encoding to use for `Bool` values.

*   `[numeric](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC12BoolEncodingO7numericyA2EmF) `
    
    Encodes `true` as `1`, `false` as `0`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[literal](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC12BoolEncodingO7literalyA2EmF) `
    
    Encodes `true` as “true”, `false` as “false”. This is the default encoding.
    
    #### Declaration

# URLEncodedFormEncoder Class Reference

URLEncodedFormEncoder
=====================

An object that encodes instances into URL-encoded query strings.

`ArrayEncoding` can be used to configure how `Array` values are encoded. By default, the `.brackets` encoding is used, encoding array values with brackets for each value. e.g `array[]=1&array[]=2`.

`BoolEncoding` can be used to configure how `Bool` values are encoded. By default, the `.numeric` encoding is used, encoding `true` as `1` and `false` as `0`.

`DataEncoding` can be used to configure how `Data` values are encoded. By default, the `.deferredToData` encoding is used, which encodes `Data` values using their default `Encodable` implementation.

`DateEncoding` can be used to configure how `Date` values are encoded. By default, the `.deferredToDate` encoding is used, which encodes `Date`s using their default `Encodable` implementation.

`KeyEncoding` can be used to configure how keys are encoded. By default, the `.useDefaultKeys` encoding is used, which encodes the keys directly from the `Encodable` implementation.

`KeyPathEncoding` can be used to configure how paths within nested objects are encoded. By default, the `.brackets` encoding is used, which encodes each sub-key in brackets. e.g. `parent[child][grandchild]=value`.

`NilEncoding` can be used to configure how `nil` `Optional` values are encoded. By default, the `.dropKey` encoding is used, which drops `nil` key / value pairs from the output entirely.

`SpaceEncoding` can be used to configure how spaces are encoded. By default, the `.percentEscaped` encoding is used, replacing spaces with `%20`.

This type is largely based on Vapor’s [`url-encoded-form`](https://github.com/vapor/url-encoded-form)
 project.

*   `[ArrayEncoding](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC13ArrayEncodingO) `
    
    Encoding to use for `Array` values.
    
    [See more](../Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder/ArrayEncoding.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[BoolEncoding](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC12BoolEncodingO) `
    
    Encoding to use for `Bool` values.
    
    [See more](../Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder/BoolEncoding.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DataEncoding](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC12DataEncodingO) `

    [See more](../Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder/DataEncoding.html)

     and [`XMLEncoder`s `KeyEncodingStrategy`](https://github.com/MaxDesiatov/XMLCoder/blob/master/Sources/XMLCoder/Encoder/XMLEncoder.swift#L102)
    .

    #### Declaration
    
*   `[KeyPathEncoding](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC15KeyPathEncodingV) `

        ["parent" : ["child" : ["grandchild": "value"]]]
        
    
    This encoding affects how the `parent`, `child`, `grandchild` path is encoded. Brackets are used by default. e.g. `parent[child][grandchild]=value`.

# ArrayEncoding Enumeration Reference

ArrayEncoding
=============

Encoding to use for `Array` values.

*   `[brackets](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC13ArrayEncodingO8bracketsyA2EmF) `
    
    An empty set of square brackets (“\[\]”) are appended to the key for every value. This is the default encoding.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[noBrackets](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC13ArrayEncodingO10noBracketsyA2EmF) `
    
    No brackets are appended to the key and the key is encoded as is.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[indexInBrackets](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC13ArrayEncodingO15indexInBracketsyA2EmF) `
    
    Brackets containing the item index are appended. This matches the jQuery and Node.js behavior.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[custom(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC13ArrayEncodingO6customyAES2S_SitccAEmF) `
    
    Provide a custom array key encoding with the given closure.
    
    #### Declaration

# KeyEncoding Enumeration Reference

KeyEncoding
===========

Encoding to use for keys.

This type is derived from [`JSONEncoder`‘s `KeyEncodingStrategy`](https://github.com/apple/swift/blob/6aa313b8dd5f05135f7f878eccc1db6f9fbe34ff/stdlib/public/Darwin/Foundation/JSONEncoder.swift#L128)
 and [`XMLEncoder`s `KeyEncodingStrategy`](https://github.com/MaxDesiatov/XMLCoder/blob/master/Sources/XMLCoder/Encoder/XMLEncoder.swift#L102)
.

*   `[useDefaultKeys](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC11KeyEncodingO14useDefaultKeysyA2EmF) `
    
    Use the keys specified by each type. This is the default encoding.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[convertToSnakeCase](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC11KeyEncodingO18convertToSnakeCaseyA2EmF) `
    
    Convert from “camelCaseKeys” to “snake\_case\_keys” before writing a key.
    
    Capital characters are determined by testing membership in `CharacterSet.uppercaseLetters` and `CharacterSet.lowercaseLetters` (Unicode General Categories Lu and Lt). The conversion to lower case uses `Locale.system`, also known as the ICU “root” locale. This means the result is consistent regardless of the current user’s locale and language preferences.
    
    Converting from camel case to snake case:
    
    1.  Splits words at the boundary of lower-case to upper-case
    2.  Inserts `_` between words
    3.  Lowercases the entire string
    4.  Preserves starting and ending `_`.
    
    For example, `oneTwoThree` becomes `one_two_three`. `_oneTwoThree_` becomes `_one_two_three_`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[convertToKebabCase](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC11KeyEncodingO18convertToKebabCaseyA2EmF) `
    
    Same as convertToSnakeCase, but using `-` instead of `_`. For example `oneTwoThree` becomes `one-two-three`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[capitalized](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC11KeyEncodingO11capitalizedyA2EmF) `
    
    Capitalize the first letter only. For example `oneTwoThree` becomes `OneTwoThree`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[uppercased](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC11KeyEncodingO10uppercasedyA2EmF) `
    
    Uppercase all letters. For example `oneTwoThree` becomes `ONETWOTHREE`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[lowercased](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC11KeyEncodingO10lowercasedyA2EmF) `
    
    Lowercase all letters. For example `oneTwoThree` becomes `onetwothree`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[custom(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC11KeyEncodingO6customyAES2SccAEmF) `
    
    A custom encoding using the provided closure.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# Destination Enumeration Reference

Destination
===========

Defines where the URL-encoded string should be set for each `URLRequest`.

*   `[methodDependent](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC11DestinationO15methodDependentyA2EmF) `
    
    Applies the encoded query string to any existing query string for `.get`, `.head`, and `.delete` request. Sets it to the `[httpBody](../../Classes/URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder/Destination.html#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC11DestinationO8httpBodyyA2EmF) ` for all other methods.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[queryString](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC11DestinationO11queryStringyA2EmF) `
    
    Applies the encoded query string to any existing query string from the `URLRequest`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[httpBody](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC11DestinationO8httpBodyyA2EmF) `
    
    Applies the encoded query string to the `httpBody` of the `URLRequest`.
    
    #### Declaration

# KeyPathEncoding Structure Reference

KeyPathEncoding
===============

Encoding to use for nested object and `Encodable` value key paths.

    ["parent" : ["child" : ["grandchild": "value"]]]
    

This encoding affects how the `parent`, `child`, `grandchild` path is encoded. Brackets are used by default. e.g. `parent[child][grandchild]=value`.

*   `[brackets](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC15KeyPathEncodingV8bracketsAEvpZ) `
    
    Encodes key paths by wrapping each component in brackets. e.g. `parent[child][grandchild]`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[dots](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC15KeyPathEncodingV4dotsAEvpZ) `
    
    Encodes key paths by separating each component with dots. e.g. `parent.child.grandchild`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(encoding:)](#/s:9Alamofire21URLEncodedFormEncoderC15KeyPathEncodingV8encodingAES2SYbc_tcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance with the encoding closure called for each sub-key in a key path.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_encoding_` | Closure used to perform the encoding. |

# URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder Class Reference

URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder
==============================

A `[ParameterEncoder](../Protocols/ParameterEncoder.html) ` that encodes types as URL-encoded query strings to be set on the URL or as body data, depending on the `Destination` set.

If no `Content-Type` header is already set on the provided `URLRequest`s, it will be set to `application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8`.

Encoding behavior can be customized by passing an instance of `[URLEncodedFormEncoder](../Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder.html) ` to the initializer.

*   `[Destination](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC11DestinationO) `
    
    Defines where the URL-encoded string should be set for each `URLRequest`.
    
    [See more](../Classes/URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder/Destination.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[default](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC7defaultACvpZ) `
    
    Returns an encoder with default parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[encoder](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC7encoderAA0bcE0Cvp) `
    
    The `[URLEncodedFormEncoder](../Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder.html) ` to use.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[destination](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC11destinationAC11DestinationOvp) `
    
    The `[Destination](../Classes/URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder/Destination.html) ` for the URL-encoded string.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(encoder:destination:)](#/s:9Alamofire30URLEncodedFormParameterEncoderC7encoder11destinationAcA0bcE0C_AC11DestinationOtcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance with the provided `[URLEncodedFormEncoder](../Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder.html) ` instance and `[Destination](../Classes/URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder/Destination.html) ` value.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_encoder_` | The `[URLEncodedFormEncoder](../Classes/URLEncodedFormEncoder.html) `. `URLEncodedFormEncoder()` by default. |
    | `_destination_` | The `[Destination](../Classes/URLEncodedFormParameterEncoder/Destination.html) `. `.methodDependent` by default. |
    
*   `[encode(_:into:)](#/s:9Alamofire16ParameterEncoderP6encode_4into10Foundation10URLRequestVqd__Sg_AHtKSERd__s8SendableRd__lF) `
    
    #### Declaration

    Upload from the provided file `URL`, as well as a `Bool` determining whether the source file should be automatically removed once uploaded.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[stream(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire13UploadRequestC10UploadableO6streamyAESo13NSInputStreamCcAEmF) `
    
    Upload from the provided `InputStream`.

# MultipartEncodingFailureReason Enumeration Reference

MultipartEncodingFailureReason
==============================

The underlying reason the `.multipartEncodingFailed` error occurred.

*   `[bodyPartURLInvalid(url:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO18bodyPartURLInvalidyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    The `fileURL` provided for reading an encodable body part isn’t a file `URL`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[bodyPartFilenameInvalid(in:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO23bodyPartFilenameInvalidyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    The filename of the `fileURL` provided has either an empty `lastPathComponent` or `pathExtension`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[bodyPartFileNotReachable(at:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO24bodyPartFileNotReachableyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    The file at the `fileURL` provided was not reachable.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[bodyPartFileNotReachableWithError(atURL:error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO33bodyPartFileNotReachableWithErroryAE10Foundation3URLV_s0M0_ptcAEmF) `
    
    Attempting to check the reachability of the `fileURL` provided threw an error.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[bodyPartFileIsDirectory(at:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO23bodyPartFileIsDirectoryyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    The file at the `fileURL` provided is actually a directory.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[bodyPartFileSizeNotAvailable(at:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO28bodyPartFileSizeNotAvailableyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    The size of the file at the `fileURL` provided was not returned by the system.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[bodyPartFileSizeQueryFailedWithError(forURL:error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO36bodyPartFileSizeQueryFailedWithErroryAE10Foundation3URLV_s0N0_ptcAEmF) `
    
    The attempt to find the size of the file at the `fileURL` provided threw an error.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[bodyPartInputStreamCreationFailed(for:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO33bodyPartInputStreamCreationFailedyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    An `InputStream` could not be created for the provided `fileURL`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[outputStreamCreationFailed(for:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO26outputStreamCreationFailedyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    An `OutputStream` could not be created when attempting to write the encoded data to disk.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[outputStreamFileAlreadyExists(at:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO29outputStreamFileAlreadyExistsyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    The encoded body data could not be written to disk because a file already exists at the provided `fileURL`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[outputStreamURLInvalid(url:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO22outputStreamURLInvalidyAE10Foundation3URLV_tcAEmF) `
    
    The `fileURL` provided for writing the encoded body data to disk is not a file `URL`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[outputStreamWriteFailed(error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO23outputStreamWriteFailedyAEs5Error_p_tcAEmF) `
    
    The attempt to write the encoded body data to disk failed with an underlying error.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[inputStreamReadFailed(error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO21inputStreamReadFailedyAEs5Error_p_tcAEmF) `
    
    The attempt to read an encoded body part `InputStream` failed with underlying system error.
    
    #### Declaration

# UnexpectedInputStreamLength Structure Reference

UnexpectedInputStreamLength
===========================

Represents unexpected input stream length that occur when encoding the `[MultipartFormData](../../Classes/MultipartFormData.html) `. Instances will be embedded within an `AFError.multipartEncodingFailed` `.inputStreamReadFailed` case.

*   `[bytesExpected](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO27UnexpectedInputStreamLengthV13bytesExpecteds6UInt64Vvp) `
    
    The expected byte count to read.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[bytesRead](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO27UnexpectedInputStreamLengthV9bytesReads6UInt64Vvp) `
    
    The actual byte count read.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# AFError Enumeration Reference

AFError
=======

`AFError` is the error type returned by Alamofire. It encompasses a few different types of errors, each with their own associated reasons.

*   `[MultipartEncodingFailureReason](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30MultipartEncodingFailureReasonO) `
    
    The underlying reason the `.multipartEncodingFailed` error occurred.
    
    [See more](../Enums/AFError/MultipartEncodingFailureReason.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[UnexpectedInputStreamLength](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO27UnexpectedInputStreamLengthV) `
    
    Represents unexpected input stream length that occur when encoding the `[MultipartFormData](../Classes/MultipartFormData.html) `. Instances will be embedded within an `AFError.multipartEncodingFailed` `.inputStreamReadFailed` case.
    
    [See more](../Enums/AFError/UnexpectedInputStreamLength.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ParameterEncodingFailureReason](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO30ParameterEncodingFailureReasonO) `
    
    The underlying reason the `.parameterEncodingFailed` error occurred.
    
    [See more](../Enums/AFError/ParameterEncodingFailureReason.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ParameterEncoderFailureReason](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO29ParameterEncoderFailureReasonO) `
    
    The underlying reason the `.parameterEncoderFailed` error occurred.
    
    [See more](../Enums/AFError/ParameterEncoderFailureReason.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ResponseValidationFailureReason](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO31ResponseValidationFailureReasonO) `
    
    The underlying reason the `.responseValidationFailed` error occurred.
    
    [See more](../Enums/AFError/ResponseValidationFailureReason.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ResponseSerializationFailureReason](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO34ResponseSerializationFailureReasonO) `
    
    The underlying reason the response serialization error occurred.
    
    [See more](../Enums/AFError/ResponseSerializationFailureReason.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ServerTrustFailureReason](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO24ServerTrustFailureReasonO) `
    
    Underlying reason a server trust evaluation error occurred.
    
    [See more](../Enums/AFError/ServerTrustFailureReason.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[URLRequestValidationFailureReason](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO33URLRequestValidationFailureReasonO) `
    
    The underlying reason the `.urlRequestValidationFailed` error occurred.
    
    [See more](../Enums/AFError/URLRequestValidationFailureReason.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[createUploadableFailed(error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO22createUploadableFailedyACs5Error_p_tcACmF) `
    
    `[UploadableConvertible](../Protocols/UploadableConvertible.html) ` threw an error in `createUploadable()`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[createURLRequestFailed(error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO22createURLRequestFailedyACs5Error_p_tcACmF) `
    
    `[URLRequestConvertible](../Protocols/URLRequestConvertible.html) ` threw an error in `asURLRequest()`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[downloadedFileMoveFailed(error:source:destination:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO24downloadedFileMoveFailedyACs5Error_p_10Foundation3URLVAHtcACmF) `
    
    `[SessionDelegate](../Classes/SessionDelegate.html) ` threw an error while attempting to move downloaded file to destination URL.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[explicitlyCancelled](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO19explicitlyCancelledyA2CmF) `
    
    `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` was explicitly cancelled.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[invalidURL(url:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO10invalidURLyAcA14URLConvertible_p_tcACmF) `
    
    `[URLConvertible](../Protocols/URLConvertible.html) ` type failed to create a valid `URL`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[multipartEncodingFailed(reason:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO23multipartEncodingFailedyA2C09MultipartD13FailureReasonO_tcACmF) `
    
    Multipart form encoding failed.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[parameterEncodingFailed(reason:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO23parameterEncodingFailedyA2C09ParameterD13FailureReasonO_tcACmF) `
    
    `[ParameterEncoding](../Protocols/ParameterEncoding.html) ` threw an error during the encoding process.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[parameterEncoderFailed(reason:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO22parameterEncoderFailedyA2C09ParameterD13FailureReasonO_tcACmF) `
    
    `[ParameterEncoder](../Protocols/ParameterEncoder.html) ` threw an error while running the encoder.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[requestAdaptationFailed(error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO23requestAdaptationFailedyACs5Error_p_tcACmF) `
    
    `[RequestAdapter](../Protocols/RequestAdapter.html) ` threw an error during adaptation.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[requestRetryFailed(retryError:originalError:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO18requestRetryFailedyACs5Error_p_sAE_ptcACmF) `
    
    `[RequestRetrier](../Protocols/RequestRetrier.html) ` threw an error during the request retry process.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[responseValidationFailed(reason:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO24responseValidationFailedyA2C08ResponseD13FailureReasonO_tcACmF) `

    #### Declaration
    
*   `[responseSerializationFailed(reason:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO27responseSerializationFailedyA2C08ResponseD13FailureReasonO_tcACmF) `

    #### Declaration
    
*   `[serverTrustEvaluationFailed(reason:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO27serverTrustEvaluationFailedyA2C06ServerD13FailureReasonO_tcACmF) `
    
    `[ServerTrustEvaluating](../Protocols/ServerTrustEvaluating.html) ` instance threw an error during trust evaluation.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[sessionDeinitialized](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO20sessionDeinitializedyA2CmF) `
    
    `[Session](../Classes/Session.html) ` which issued the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` was deinitialized, most likely because its reference went out of scope.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[sessionInvalidated(error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO18sessionInvalidatedyACs5Error_pSg_tcACmF) `
    
    `[Session](../Classes/Session.html) ` was explicitly invalidated, possibly with the `Error` produced by the underlying `URLSession`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[sessionTaskFailed(error:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO17sessionTaskFailedyACs5Error_p_tcACmF) `
    
    `URLSessionTask` completed with error.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[urlRequestValidationFailed(reason:)](#/s:9Alamofire7AFErrorO26urlRequestValidationFailedyA2C010URLRequestE13FailureReasonO_tcACmF) `
    
    `URLRequest` failed validation.
    
    #### Declaration

# CharacterSet Extension Reference

CharacterSet
============

*   `[afURLQueryAllowed](#/s:10Foundation12CharacterSetV9AlamofireE17afURLQueryAllowedACvpZ) `
    
    Creates a CharacterSet from RFC 3986 allowed characters.
    
    RFC 3986 states that the following characters are “reserved” characters.
    
    *   General Delimiters: “:”, “#”, “\[”, “\]”, “@”, “?”, “/”
    *   Sub-Delimiters: “!”, “$”, “&”, “‘”, “(”, “)”, “\*”, “+”, “,”, “;”, “=”
    
    In RFC 3986 - Section 3.4, it states that the “?” and “/” characters should not be escaped to allow query strings to include a URL. Therefore, all “reserved” characters with the exception of “?” and “/” should be percent-escaped in the query string.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# AuthenticationError Enumeration Reference

AuthenticationError
===================

Represents various authentication failures that occur when using the `[AuthenticationInterceptor](../Classes/AuthenticationInterceptor.html) `. All errors are still vended from Alamofire as `[AFError](../Enums/AFError.html) ` types. The `AuthenticationError` instances will be embedded within `[AFError](../Enums/AFError.html) ` `.requestAdaptationFailed` or `.requestRetryFailed` cases.

*   `[missingCredential](#/s:9Alamofire19AuthenticationErrorO17missingCredentialyA2CmF) `
    
    The credential was missing so the request could not be authenticated.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[excessiveRefresh](#/s:9Alamofire19AuthenticationErrorO16excessiveRefreshyA2CmF) `
    
    The credential was refreshed too many times within the `RefreshWindow`.
    
    #### Declaration

---

[](#/Protocol%20Conformances)

### Protocol Conformances

*   `[RequestDelegate](#/s:9Alamofire15RequestDelegateP) `
