    [See more](Protocols/RequestDelegate.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[URLConvertible](#/s:9Alamofire14URLConvertibleP) `
    
    Types adopting the `URLConvertible` protocol can be used to construct `URL`s, which can then be used to construct `URLRequest`s.
    
    [See more](Protocols/URLConvertible.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

*   `[URLRequestConvertible](#/s:9Alamofire21URLRequestConvertibleP) `
    
    Types adopting the `URLRequestConvertible` protocol can be used to safely construct `URLRequest`s.
    
    [See more](Protocols/URLRequestConvertible.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[UploadableConvertible](#/s:9Alamofire21UploadableConvertibleP) `
    
    A type that can produce an `[UploadRequest.Uploadable](Classes/UploadRequest/Uploadable.html) ` value.
    
    [See more](Protocols/UploadableConvertible.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[UploadConvertible](#/s:9Alamofire17UploadConvertibleP) `
    
    A type that can be converted to an upload, whether from an `[UploadRequest.Uploadable](Classes/UploadRequest/Uploadable.html) ` or `[URLRequestConvertible](Protocols/URLRequestConvertible.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[WebSocketMessageSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire26WebSocketMessageSerializerP) `
    
    Undocumented
    
    [See more](Protocols/WebSocketMessageSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[AlamofireExtended](#/s:9Alamofire0A8ExtendedP) `
    
    Protocol describing the `af` extension points for Alamofire extended types.
    
    [See more](Protocols/AlamofireExtended.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[AuthenticationCredential](#/s:9Alamofire24AuthenticationCredentialP) `
    
    Types adopting the `AuthenticationCredential` protocol can be used to authenticate `URLRequest`s.
    
    One common example of an `AuthenticationCredential` is an OAuth2 credential containing an access token used to authenticate all requests on behalf of a user. The access token generally has an expiration window of 60 minutes which will then require a refresh of the credential using the refresh token to generate a new access token.
    
    [See more](Protocols/AuthenticationCredential.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Authenticator](#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP) `
    
    Types adopting the `Authenticator` protocol can be used to authenticate `URLRequest`s with an `[AuthenticationCredential](Protocols/AuthenticationCredential.html) ` as well as refresh the `[AuthenticationCredential](Protocols/AuthenticationCredential.html) ` when required.
    
    [See more](Protocols/Authenticator.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[CachedResponseHandler](#/s:9Alamofire21CachedResponseHandlerP) `
    
    A type that handles whether the data task should store the HTTP response in the cache.
    
    [See more](Protocols/CachedResponseHandler.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[EventMonitor](#/s:9Alamofire12EventMonitorP) `
    
    Protocol outlining the lifetime events inside Alamofire. It includes both events received from the various `URLSession` delegate protocols as well as various events from the lifetime of `[Request](Classes/Request.html) ` and its subclasses.
    
    [See more](Protocols/EventMonitor.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[RedirectHandler](#/s:9Alamofire15RedirectHandlerP) `
    
    A type that handles how an HTTP redirect response from a remote server should be redirected to the new request.
    
    [See more](Protocols/RedirectHandler.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[RequestInterceptor](#/s:9Alamofire18RequestInterceptorP) `
    
    Type that provides both `[RequestAdapter](Protocols/RequestAdapter.html) ` and `[RequestRetrier](Protocols/RequestRetrier.html) ` functionality.
    
    [See more](Protocols/RequestInterceptor.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[RequestAdapter](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestAdapterP) `
    
    A type that can inspect and optionally adapt a `URLRequest` in some manner if necessary.
    
    [See more](Protocols/RequestAdapter.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[RequestRetrier](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestRetrierP) `
    
    A type that determines whether a request should be retried after being executed by the specified session manager and encountering an error.
    
    [See more](Protocols/RequestRetrier.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DataResponseSerializerProtocol](#/s:9Alamofire30DataResponseSerializerProtocolP) `
    
    The type to which all data response serializers must conform in order to serialize a response.
    
    [See more](Protocols/DataResponseSerializerProtocol.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DownloadResponseSerializerProtocol](#/s:9Alamofire34DownloadResponseSerializerProtocolP) `
    
    The type to which all download response serializers must conform in order to serialize a response.
    
    [See more](Protocols/DownloadResponseSerializerProtocol.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ResponseSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP) `
    
    A serializer that can handle both data and download responses.
    
    [See more](Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DataPreprocessor](#/s:9Alamofire16DataPreprocessorP) `
    
    Type used to preprocess `Data` before it handled by a serializer.
    
    [See more](Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html)
    
    #### Declaration

# CachedResponseHandler Protocol Reference

CachedResponseHandler
=====================

A type that handles whether the data task should store the HTTP response in the cache.

*   `[dataTask(_:willCacheResponse:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire21CachedResponseHandlerP8dataTask_09willCacheC010completionySo016NSURLSessionDataF0C_So19NSCachedURLResponseCyAJSgctF) `
    
    Determines whether the HTTP response should be stored in the cache.
    
    The `completion` closure should be passed one of three possible options:
    
    1.  The cached response provided by the server (this is the most common use case).
    2.  A modified version of the cached response (you may want to modify it in some way before caching).
    3.  A `nil` value to prevent the cached response from being stored in the cache.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_task_` | The data task whose request resulted in the cached response. |
    | `_response_` | The cached response to potentially store in the cache. |
    | `_completion_` | The closure to execute containing cached response, a modified response, or `nil`. |
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60Self%60%20%3D%3D%20%60ResponseCacher%60)

### Available where `Self` == `[ResponseCacher](../Structs/ResponseCacher.html) `

*   `[cache](#/s:9Alamofire21CachedResponseHandlerPA2A0C6CacherVRszrlE5cacheAEvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Provides a `[ResponseCacher](../Structs/ResponseCacher.html) ` which caches the response, if allowed. Equivalent to `[ResponseCacher.cache](../Structs/ResponseCacher.html#/s:9Alamofire14ResponseCacherV5cacheACvpZ) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[doNotCache](#/s:9Alamofire21CachedResponseHandlerPA2A0C6CacherVRszrlE10doNotCacheAEvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Provides a `[ResponseCacher](../Structs/ResponseCacher.html) ` which does not cache the response. Equivalent to `[ResponseCacher.doNotCache](../Structs/ResponseCacher.html#/s:9Alamofire14ResponseCacherV10doNotCacheACvpZ) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[modify(using:)](#/s:9Alamofire21CachedResponseHandlerPA2A0C6CacherVRszrlE6modify5usingAESo19NSCachedURLResponseCSgSo20NSURLSessionDataTaskC_AItYbc_tFZ)` Extension method
    
    Creates a `[ResponseCacher](../Structs/ResponseCacher.html) ` which modifies the proposed `CachedURLResponse` using the provided closure.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_closure_` | Closure used to modify the `CachedURLResponse`. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[ResponseCacher](../Structs/ResponseCacher.html) `.

---

# Authenticator Protocol Reference

Authenticator
=============

Types adopting the `Authenticator` protocol can be used to authenticate `URLRequest`s with an `[AuthenticationCredential](../Protocols/AuthenticationCredential.html) ` as well as refresh the `[AuthenticationCredential](../Protocols/AuthenticationCredential.html) ` when required.

*   `[Credential](#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `
    
    The type of credential associated with the `Authenticator` instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[apply(_:to:)](#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP5apply_2toy10CredentialQz_10Foundation10URLRequestVztF) `
    
    Applies the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) ` to the `URLRequest`.
    
    In the case of OAuth2, the access token of the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) ` would be added to the `URLRequest` as a Bearer token to the `Authorization` header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_credential_` | The `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `. |
    | `_urlRequest_` | The `URLRequest`. |
    
*   `[refresh(_:for:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP7refresh_3for10completiony10CredentialQz_AA7SessionCys6ResultOyAHs5Error_pGYbctF) `
    
    Refreshes the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) ` and executes the `completion` closure with the `Result` once complete.
    
    Refresh can be called in one of two ways. It can be called before the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` is actually executed due to a `requiresRefresh` returning `true` during the adapt portion of the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` creation process. It can also be triggered by a failed `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` where the authentication server denied access due to an expired or invalidated access token.
    
    In the case of OAuth2, this method would use the refresh token of the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) ` to generate a new `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) ` using the authentication service. Once complete, the `completion` closure should be called with the new `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `, or the error that occurred.
    
    In general, if the refresh call fails with certain status codes from the authentication server (commonly a 401), the refresh token in the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) ` can no longer be used to generate a valid `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `. In these cases, you will need to reauthenticate the user with their username / password.
    
    Please note, these are just general examples of common use cases. They are not meant to solve your specific authentication server challenges. Please work with your authentication server team to ensure your `Authenticator` logic matches their expectations.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_credential_` | The `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) ` to refresh. |
    | `_session_` | The `[Session](../Classes/Session.html) ` requiring the refresh. |
    | `_completion_` | The closure to be executed once the refresh is complete. |
    
*   `[didRequest(_:with:failDueToAuthenticationError:)](#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10didRequest_4with28failDueToAuthenticationErrorSb10Foundation10URLRequestV_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCs0J0_ptF) `
    
    Determines whether the `URLRequest` failed due to an authentication error based on the `HTTPURLResponse`.
    
    If the authentication server **CANNOT** invalidate credentials after they are issued, then simply return `false` for this method. If the authentication server **CAN** invalidate credentials due to security breaches, then you will need to work with your authentication server team to understand how to identify when this occurs.
    
    In the case of OAuth2, where an authentication server can invalidate credentials, you will need to inspect the `HTTPURLResponse` or possibly the `Error` for when this occurs. This is commonly handled by the authentication server returning a 401 status code and some additional header to indicate an OAuth2 failure occurred.
    
    It is very important to understand how your authentication server works to be able to implement this correctly. For example, if your authentication server returns a 401 when an OAuth2 error occurs, and your downstream service also returns a 401 when you are not authorized to perform that operation, how do you know which layer of the backend returned you a 401? You do not want to trigger a refresh unless you know your authentication server is actually the layer rejecting the request. Again, work with your authentication server team to understand how to identify an OAuth2 401 error vs. a downstream 401 error to avoid endless refresh loops.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_urlRequest_` | The `URLRequest`. |
    | `_response_` | The `HTTPURLResponse`. |
    | `_error_` | The `Error`. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    `true` if the `URLRequest` failed due to an authentication error, `false` otherwise.
    
*   `[isRequest(_:authenticatedWith:)](#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP9isRequest_17authenticatedWithSb10Foundation10URLRequestV_10CredentialQztF) `
    
    Determines whether the `URLRequest` is authenticated with the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `.
    
    If the authentication server **CANNOT** invalidate credentials after they are issued, then simply return `true` for this method. If the authentication server **CAN** invalidate credentials due to security breaches, then read on.
    
    When an authentication server can invalidate credentials, it means that you may have a non-expired credential that appears to be valid, but will be rejected by the authentication server when used. Generally when this happens, a number of requests are all sent when the application is foregrounded, and all of them will be rejected by the authentication server in the order they are received. The first failed request will trigger a refresh internally, which will update the credential, and then retry all the queued requests with the new credential. However, it is possible that some of the original requests will not return from the authentication server until the refresh has completed. This is where this method comes in.
    
    When the authentication server rejects a credential, we need to check to make sure we haven’t refreshed the credential while the request was in flight. If it has already refreshed, then we don’t need to trigger an additional refresh. If it hasn’t refreshed, then we need to refresh.
    
    Now that it is understood how the result of this method is used in the refresh lifecycle, let’s walk through how to implement it. You should return `true` in this method if the `URLRequest` is authenticated in a way that matches the values in the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `. In the case of OAuth2, this would mean that the Bearer token in the `Authorization` header of the `URLRequest` matches the access token in the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `. If it matches, then we know the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) ` was used to authenticate the `URLRequest` and should return `true`. If the Bearer token did not match the access token, then you should return `false`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_urlRequest_` | The `URLRequest`. |
    | `_credential_` | The `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    `true` if the `URLRequest` is authenticated with the `[Credential](../Protocols/Authenticator.html#/s:9Alamofire13AuthenticatorP10CredentialQa) `, `false` otherwise.

---

# AuthenticationCredential Protocol Reference

AuthenticationCredential
========================

Types adopting the `AuthenticationCredential` protocol can be used to authenticate `URLRequest`s.

One common example of an `AuthenticationCredential` is an OAuth2 credential containing an access token used to authenticate all requests on behalf of a user. The access token generally has an expiration window of 60 minutes which will then require a refresh of the credential using the refresh token to generate a new access token.

*   `[requiresRefresh](#/s:9Alamofire24AuthenticationCredentialP15requiresRefreshSbvp) `
    
    Whether the credential requires a refresh. This property should always return `true` when the credential is expired. It is also wise to consider returning `true` when the credential will expire in several seconds or minutes depending on the expiration window of the credential.
    
    For example, if the credential is valid for 60 minutes, then it would be wise to return `true` when the credential is only valid for 5 minutes or less. That ensures the credential will not expire as it is passed around backend services.
    
    #### Declaration

---

# RedirectHandler Protocol Reference

RedirectHandler
===============

A type that handles how an HTTP redirect response from a remote server should be redirected to the new request.

*   `[task(_:willBeRedirectedTo:for:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire15RedirectHandlerP4task_18willBeRedirectedTo3for10completionySo16NSURLSessionTaskC_10Foundation10URLRequestVSo17NSHTTPURLResponseCyALSgctF) `
    
    Determines how the HTTP redirect response should be redirected to the new request.
    
    The `completion` closure should be passed one of three possible options:
    
    1.  The new request specified by the redirect (this is the most common use case).
    2.  A modified version of the new request (you may want to route it somewhere else).
    3.  A `nil` value to deny the redirect request and return the body of the redirect response.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_task_` | The `URLSessionTask` whose request resulted in a redirect. |
    | `_request_` | The `URLRequest` to the new location specified by the redirect response. |
    | `_response_` | The `HTTPURLResponse` containing the server’s response to the original request. |
    | `_completion_` | The closure to execute containing the new `URLRequest`, a modified `URLRequest`, or `nil`. |
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60Self%60%20%3D%3D%20%60Redirector%60)

### Available where `Self` == `[Redirector](../Structs/Redirector.html) `

*   `[follow](#/s:9Alamofire15RedirectHandlerPA2A10RedirectorVRszrlE6followAEvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Provides a `[Redirector](../Structs/Redirector.html) ` which follows redirects. Equivalent to `[Redirector.follow](../Structs/Redirector.html#/s:9Alamofire10RedirectorV6followACvpZ) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[doNotFollow](#/s:9Alamofire15RedirectHandlerPA2A10RedirectorVRszrlE11doNotFollowAEvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Provides a `[Redirector](../Structs/Redirector.html) ` which does not follow redirects. Equivalent to `[Redirector.doNotFollow](../Structs/Redirector.html#/s:9Alamofire10RedirectorV11doNotFollowACvpZ) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[modify(using:)](#/s:9Alamofire15RedirectHandlerPA2A10RedirectorVRszrlE6modify5usingAE10Foundation10URLRequestVSgSo16NSURLSessionTaskC_AJSo17NSHTTPURLResponseCtYbc_tFZ)` Extension method
    
    Creates a `[Redirector](../Structs/Redirector.html) ` which modifies the redirected `URLRequest` using the provided closure.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_closure_` | Closure used to modify the redirect. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[Redirector](../Structs/Redirector.html) `.

---

# RequestRetrier Protocol Reference

RequestRetrier
==============

A type that determines whether a request should be retried after being executed by the specified session manager and encountering an error.

*   `[retry(_:for:dueTo:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestRetrierP5retry_3for5dueTo10completionyAA0B0C_AA7SessionCs5Error_pyAA11RetryResultOYbctF) `
    
    Determines whether the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` should be retried by calling the `completion` closure.
    
    This operation is fully asynchronous. Any amount of time can be taken to determine whether the request needs to be retried. The one requirement is that the completion closure is called to ensure the request is properly cleaned up after.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` that failed due to the provided `Error`. |
    | `_session_` | `[Session](../Classes/Session.html) ` that produced the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `. |
    | `_error_` | `Error` encountered while executing the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `. |
    | `_completion_` | Completion closure to be executed when a retry decision has been determined. |
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60Self%60%20%3D%3D%20%60Retrier%60)

### Available where `Self` == `[Retrier](../Classes/Retrier.html) `

*   `[retrier(using:)](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestRetrierPA2A0C0CRszrlE7retrier5usingAEyAA0B0C_AA7SessionCs5Error_pyAA11RetryResultOctc_tFZ)` Extension method
    
    Creates a `[Retrier](../Classes/Retrier.html) ` using the provided `[RetryHandler](../Typealiases.html#/s:9Alamofire12RetryHandlera) ` closure.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_closure_` | `[RetryHandler](../Typealiases.html#/s:9Alamofire12RetryHandlera) ` to use to retry the request. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[Retrier](../Classes/Retrier.html) `.

---

# RequestAdapter Protocol Reference

RequestAdapter
==============

A type that can inspect and optionally adapt a `URLRequest` in some manner if necessary.

*   `[adapt(_:for:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestAdapterP5adapt_3for10completiony10Foundation10URLRequestV_AA7SessionCys6ResultOyAIs5Error_pGYbctF) `
    
    Inspects and adapts the specified `URLRequest` in some manner and calls the completion handler with the Result.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_urlRequest_` | The `URLRequest` to adapt. |
    | `_session_` | The `[Session](../Classes/Session.html) ` that will execute the `URLRequest`. |
    | `_completion_` | The completion handler that must be called when adaptation is complete. |
    
*   `[adapt(_:using:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestAdapterP5adapt_5using10completiony10Foundation10URLRequestV_AA0bC5StateVys6ResultOyAIs5Error_pGYbctF)` Default implementation
    
    Inspects and adapts the specified `URLRequest` in some manner and calls the completion handler with the Result.
    
    #### Default Implementation
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_urlRequest_` | The `URLRequest` to adapt. |
    | `_state_` | The `[RequestAdapterState](../Structs/RequestAdapterState.html) ` associated with the `URLRequest`. |
    | `_completion_` | The completion handler that must be called when adaptation is complete. |
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60Self%60%20%3D%3D%20%60Adapter%60)

### Available where `Self` == `[Adapter](../Classes/Adapter.html) `

*   `[adapter(using:)](#/s:9Alamofire14RequestAdapterPA2A0C0CRszrlE7adapter5usingAEy10Foundation10URLRequestV_AA7SessionCys6ResultOyAJs5Error_pGctc_tFZ)` Extension method
    
    Creates an `[Adapter](../Classes/Adapter.html) ` using the provided `[AdaptHandler](../Typealiases.html#/s:9Alamofire12AdaptHandlera) ` closure.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_closure_` | `[AdaptHandler](../Typealiases.html#/s:9Alamofire12AdaptHandlera) ` to use to adapt the request. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[Adapter](../Classes/Adapter.html) `.

# URLConvertible Protocol Reference

URLConvertible
==============

Types adopting the `URLConvertible` protocol can be used to construct `URL`s, which can then be used to construct `URLRequest`s.

*   `[asURL()](#/s:9Alamofire14URLConvertibleP5asURL10Foundation0D0VyKF) `
    
    Returns a `URL` from the conforming instance or throws.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `URL` created from the instance.

# ResponseSerializer Protocol Reference

ResponseSerializer
==================

A serializer that can handle both data and download responses.

*   `[dataPreprocessor](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP16dataPreprocessorAA04DataE0_pvp)` Default implementation
    
    `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) ` used to prepare incoming `Data` for serialization.
    
    #### Default Implementation
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[emptyRequestMethods](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP19emptyRequestMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvp)` Default implementation
    
    `[HTTPMethod](../Structs/HTTPMethod.html) `s for which empty response bodies are considered appropriate.
    
    #### Default Implementation
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[emptyResponseCodes](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerP05emptyB5CodesShySiGvp)` Default implementation
    
    HTTP response codes for which empty response bodies are considered appropriate.
    
    #### Default Implementation
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultDataPreprocessor](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPAAE23defaultDataPreprocessorAA0eF0_pvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Default `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) `. `[PassthroughPreprocessor](../Structs/PassthroughPreprocessor.html) ` by default.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultEmptyRequestMethods](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPAAE26defaultEmptyRequestMethodsShyAA10HTTPMethodVGvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Default `[HTTPMethod](../Structs/HTTPMethod.html) `s for which empty response bodies are always considered appropriate. `[.head]` by default.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultEmptyResponseCodes](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPAAE012defaultEmptyB5CodesShySiGvpZ)` Extension method
    
    HTTP response codes for which empty response bodies are always considered appropriate. `[204, 205]` by default.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[requestAllowsEmptyResponseData(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPAAE018requestAllowsEmptyB4DataySbSg10Foundation10URLRequestVSgF)` Extension method
    
    Determines whether the `request` allows empty response bodies, if `request` exists.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | `URLRequest` to evaluate. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    `Bool` representing the outcome of the evaluation, or `nil` if `request` was `nil`.
    
*   `[responseAllowsEmptyResponseData(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPAAE019responseAllowsEmptyB4DataySbSgSo17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgF)` Extension method
    
    Determines whether the `response` allows empty response bodies, if `response` exists.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_response_` | `HTTPURLResponse` to evaluate. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    `Bool` representing the outcome of the evaluation, or `nil` if `response` was `nil`.
    
*   `[emptyResponseAllowed(forRequest:response:)](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPAAE05emptyB7Allowed10forRequest8responseSb10Foundation10URLRequestVSg_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgtF)` Extension method
    
    Determines whether `request` and `response` allow empty response bodies.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | `URLRequest` to evaluate. |
    | `_response_` | `HTTPURLResponse` to evaluate. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    `true` if `request` or `response` allow empty bodies, `false` otherwise.
    

[](#/Decodable)

### Decodable

*   `[decodable(of:dataPreprocessor:decoder:emptyResponseCodes:emptyRequestMethods:)](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPAAE9decodable2of16dataPreprocessor7decoder05emptyB5Codes0I14RequestMethodsAA09DecodablebC0Cyqd__Gqd__m_AA04DataG0_pAA0N7Decoder_pShySiGShyAA10HTTPMethodVGtALRszSeRd__s8SendableRd__lFZ)` Extension method

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters

    | `_dataPreprocessor_` | `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) ` used to prepare the received `Data` for serialization. |
    | `_decoder_` | The `[DataDecoder](../Protocols/DataDecoder.html) `. `JSONDecoder()` by default. |
    | `_emptyResponseCodes_` | The HTTP response codes for which empty responses are allowed. `[204, 205]` by default. |
    | `_emptyRequestMethods_` | The HTTP request methods for which empty responses are allowed. `[.head]` by default. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[DecodableResponseSerializer](../Classes/DecodableResponseSerializer.html) `.

    | --- | --- |
    | `_dataPreprocessor_` | `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) ` used to prepare the received `Data` for serialization. |
    | `_emptyResponseCodes_` | The HTTP response codes for which empty responses are allowed. `[204, 205]` by default. |
    | `_emptyRequestMethods_` | The HTTP request methods for which empty responses are allowed. `[.head]` by default. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[DataResponseSerializer](../Classes/DataResponseSerializer.html) `.
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60Self%60%20%3D%3D%20%60StringResponseSerializer%60)

### Available where `Self` == `[StringResponseSerializer](../Classes/StringResponseSerializer.html) `

*   `[string](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPA2A06StringbC0CRszrlE6stringAEvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Provides a default `[StringResponseSerializer](../Classes/StringResponseSerializer.html) ` instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[string(dataPreprocessor:encoding:emptyResponseCodes:emptyRequestMethods:)](#/s:9Alamofire18ResponseSerializerPA2A06StringbC0CRszrlE6string16dataPreprocessor8encoding05emptyB5Codes0I14RequestMethodsAeA04DataG0_p_SS10FoundationE8EncodingVSgShySiGShyAA10HTTPMethodVGtFZ)` Extension method
    
    Creates a `[StringResponseSerializer](../Classes/StringResponseSerializer.html) ` with the provided values.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_dataPreprocessor_` | `[DataPreprocessor](../Protocols/DataPreprocessor.html) ` used to prepare the received `Data` for serialization. |
    | `_encoding_` | A string encoding. Defaults to `nil`, in which case the encoding will be determined from the server response, falling back to the default HTTP character set, `ISO-8859-1`. |
    | `_emptyResponseCodes_` | The HTTP response codes for which empty responses are allowed. `[204, 205]` by default. |
    | `_emptyRequestMethods_` | The HTTP request methods for which empty responses are allowed. `[.head]` by default. |

# URLRequestConvertible Protocol Reference

URLRequestConvertible
=====================

Types adopting the `URLRequestConvertible` protocol can be used to safely construct `URLRequest`s.

*   `[asURLRequest()](#/s:9Alamofire21URLRequestConvertibleP02asB010Foundation0B0VyKF) `
    
    Returns a `URLRequest` or throws if an `Error` was encountered.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A `URLRequest`.
    
*   `[urlRequest](#/s:9Alamofire21URLRequestConvertiblePAAE10urlRequest10Foundation0B0VSgvp)` Extension method
    
    The `URLRequest` returned by discarding any `Error` encountered.
    
    #### Declaration

# RequestDelegate Protocol Reference

RequestDelegate
===============

Protocol abstraction for `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `‘s communication back to the `[SessionDelegate](../Classes/SessionDelegate.html) `.

*   `[sessionConfiguration](#/s:9Alamofire15RequestDelegateP20sessionConfigurationSo012NSURLSessionE0Cvp) `
    
    `URLSessionConfiguration` used to create the underlying `URLSessionTask`s.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[startImmediately](#/s:9Alamofire15RequestDelegateP16startImmediatelySbvp) `
    
    Determines whether the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` should automatically call `resume()` when adding the first response handler.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[cleanup(after:)](#/s:9Alamofire15RequestDelegateP7cleanup5afteryAA0B0C_tF) `
    
    Notifies the delegate the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` has reached a point where it needs cleanup.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | The `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` to cleanup after. |
    
*   `[retryResult(for:dueTo:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire15RequestDelegateP11retryResult3for5dueTo10completionyAA0B0C_AA7AFErrorOyAA05RetryE0OYbctF) `
    
    Asynchronously ask the delegate whether a `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` will be retried.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` which failed. |
    | `_error_` | `Error` which produced the failure. |
    | `_completion_` | Closure taking the `[RetryResult](../Enums/RetryResult.html) ` for evaluation. |
    
*   `[retryRequest(_:withDelay:)](#/s:9Alamofire15RequestDelegateP05retryB0_9withDelayyAA0B0C_SdSgtF) `
    
    Asynchronously retry the `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | `[Request](../Classes/Request.html) ` which will be retried. |
    | `_timeDelay_` | `TimeInterval` after which the retry will be triggered. |

# ServerTrustEvaluating Protocol Reference

ServerTrustEvaluating
=====================

A protocol describing the API used to evaluate server trusts.

*   `[evaluate(_:forHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingP8evaluate_7forHostySo03SecC3Refa_SStKF) `
    
    Evaluates the given `SecTrust` value for the given `host`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_trust_` | The `SecTrust` value to evaluate. |
    | `_host_` | The host for which to evaluate the `SecTrust` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A `Bool` indicating whether the evaluator considers the `SecTrust` value valid for `host`.
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60Self%60%20%3D%3D%20%60RevocationTrustEvaluator%60)

### Available where `Self` == `[RevocationTrustEvaluator](../Classes/RevocationTrustEvaluator.html) `

*   `[revocationChecking](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingPA2A010RevocationC9EvaluatorCRszrlE18revocationCheckingAEvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Provides a default `[RevocationTrustEvaluator](../Classes/RevocationTrustEvaluator.html) ` instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[revocationChecking(performDefaultValidation:validateHost:options:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingPA2A010RevocationC9EvaluatorCRszrlE18revocationChecking24performDefaultValidation12validateHost7optionsAESb_SbAE7OptionsVtFZ)` Extension method
    
    Creates a `[RevocationTrustEvaluator](../Classes/RevocationTrustEvaluator.html) ` using the provided parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_performDefaultValidation_` | Determines whether default validation should be performed in addition to evaluating the pinned certificates. `true` by default. |
    | `_validateHost_` | Determines whether or not the evaluator should validate the host, in addition to performing the default evaluation, even if `performDefaultValidation` is `false`. `true` by default. |
    | `_options_` | The `Options` to use to check the revocation status of the certificate. `.any` by default. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[RevocationTrustEvaluator](../Classes/RevocationTrustEvaluator.html) `.
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60Self%60%20%3D%3D%20%60PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator%60)

### Available where `Self` == `[PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator](../Classes/PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator.html) `

*   `[pinnedCertificates](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingPA2A018PinnedCertificatesC9EvaluatorCRszrlE06pinnedF0AEvpZ)` Extension method
    
    Provides a default `[PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator](../Classes/PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator.html) ` instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[pinnedCertificates(certificates:acceptSelfSignedCertificates:performDefaultValidation:validateHost:)](#/s:9Alamofire21ServerTrustEvaluatingPA2A018PinnedCertificatesC9EvaluatorCRszrlE06pinnedF012certificates016acceptSelfSignedF024performDefaultValidation12validateHostAESaySo17SecCertificateRefaG_S3btFZ)` Extension method
    
    Creates a `[PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator](../Classes/PinnedCertificatesTrustEvaluator.html) ` using the provided parameters.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_certificates_` | The certificates to use to evaluate the trust. All `cer`, `crt`, and `der` certificates in `Bundle.main` by default. |
    | `_acceptSelfSignedCertificates_` | Adds the provided certificates as anchors for the trust evaluation, allowing self-signed certificates to pass. `false` by default. THIS SETTING SHOULD BE FALSE IN PRODUCTION! |
    | `_performDefaultValidation_` | Determines whether default validation should be performed in addition to evaluating the pinned certificates. `true` by default. |
    | `_validateHost_` | Determines whether or not the evaluator should validate the host, in addition to performing the default evaluation, even if `performDefaultValidation` is `false`. `true` by default. |
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60Self%60%20%3D%3D%20%60PublicKeysTrustEvaluator%60)

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |

    | `_keys_` | The `SecKey`s to use to validate public keys. Defaults to the public keys of all certificates included in the main bundle. |
    | `_performDefaultValidation_` | Determines whether default validation should be performed in addition to evaluating the pinned certificates. `true` by default. |
    | `_validateHost_` | Determines whether or not the evaluator should validate the host, in addition to performing the default evaluation, even if `performDefaultValidation` is `false`. `true` by default. |

    | `_interceptors_` | `RequestInterceptor`s to use to intercept the request. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `[Interceptor](../Classes/Interceptor.html) `.

# Structures  Reference

Structures
==========

The following structures are available globally.

### Serialization

*   `[DecodableStreamSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire25DecodableStreamSerializerV) `

    [See more](Structs/DecodableStreamSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[PassthroughStreamSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire27PassthroughStreamSerializerV) `

    [See more](Structs/PassthroughStreamSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[StringStreamSerializer](#/s:9Alamofire22StringStreamSerializerV) `
    
    `[DataStreamSerializer](Protocols/DataStreamSerializer.html) ` which serializes incoming stream `Data` into `UTF8`\-decoded `String` values.
    
    [See more](Structs/StringStreamSerializer.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[HTTPHeaders](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV) `
    
    An order-preserving and case-insensitive representation of HTTP headers.
    
    [See more](Structs/HTTPHeaders.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/HTTPHeader)

### HTTPHeader

*   `[HTTPHeader](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV) `
    
    A representation of a single HTTP header’s name / value pair.
    
    [See more](Structs/HTTPHeader.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[HTTPMethod](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV) `
    
    Type representing HTTP methods. Raw `String` value is stored and compared case-sensitively, so `HTTPMethod.get != HTTPMethod(rawValue: "get")`.
    
    See [https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-4.3](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-4.3)
    
    [See more](Structs/HTTPMethod.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

*   `[URLEncoding](#/s:9Alamofire11URLEncodingV) `
    
    Creates a url-encoded query string to be set as or appended to any existing URL query string or set as the HTTP body of the URL request. Whether the query string is set or appended to any existing URL query string or set as the HTTP body depends on the destination of the encoding.
    
    The `Content-Type` HTTP header field of an encoded request with HTTP body is set to `application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8`.
    
    There is no published specification for how to encode collection types. By default the convention of appending `[]` to the key for array values (`foo[]=1&foo[]=2`), and appending the key surrounded by square brackets for nested dictionary values (`foo[bar]=baz`) is used. Optionally, `ArrayEncoding` can be used to omit the square brackets appended to array keys.
    
    `BoolEncoding` can be used to configure how boolean values are encoded. The default behavior is to encode `true` as 1 and `false` as 0.
    
    [See more](Structs/URLEncoding.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[JSONEncoding](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV) `
    
    Uses `JSONSerialization` to create a JSON representation of the parameters object, which is set as the body of the request. The `Content-Type` HTTP header field of an encoded request is set to `application/json`.
    
    [See more](Structs/JSONEncoding.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DataResponse](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV) `
    
    Type used to store all values associated with a serialized response of a `[DataRequest](Classes/DataRequest.html) ` or `[UploadRequest](Classes/UploadRequest.html) `.
    
    [See more](Structs/DataResponse.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DownloadResponse](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV) `
    
    Used to store all data associated with a serialized response of a download request.
    
    [See more](Structs/DownloadResponse.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[DecodableWebSocketMessageDecoder](#/s:9Alamofire32DecodableWebSocketMessageDecoderV) `
    
    Undocumented
    
    [See more](Structs/DecodableWebSocketMessageDecoder.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[AlamofireExtension](#/s:9Alamofire0A9ExtensionV) `
    
    Type that acts as a generic extension point for all `[AlamofireExtended](Protocols/AlamofireExtended.html) ` types.
    
    [See more](Structs/AlamofireExtension.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ResponseCacher](#/s:9Alamofire14ResponseCacherV) `
    
    `ResponseCacher` is a convenience `[CachedResponseHandler](Protocols/CachedResponseHandler.html) ` making it easy to cache, not cache, or modify a cached response.
    
    [See more](Structs/ResponseCacher.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/DataRequest%20%2F%20UploadRequest)

# DataResponse Structure Reference

DataResponse
============

Type used to store all values associated with a serialized response of a `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) ` or `[UploadRequest](../Classes/UploadRequest.html) `.

*   `[request](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV7request10Foundation10URLRequestVSgvp) `
    
    The URL request sent to the server.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[response](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV8responseSo17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgvp) `
    
    The server’s response to the URL request.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[data](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV4data10Foundation0B0VSgvp) `
    
    The data returned by the server.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[metrics](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV7metricsSo23NSURLSessionTaskMetricsCSgvp) `
    
    The final metrics of the response.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[serializationDuration](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV21serializationDurationSdvp) `
    
    The time taken to serialize the response.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[result](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV6results6ResultOyxq_Gvp) `
    
    The result of response serialization.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[value](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV5valuexSgvp) `
    
    Returns the associated value of the result if it is a success, `nil` otherwise.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[error](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV5errorq_Sgvp) `
    
    Returns the associated error value if the result if it is a failure, `nil` otherwise.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(request:response:data:metrics:serializationDuration:result:)](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV7request8response4data7metrics21serializationDuration6resultACyxq_G10Foundation10URLRequestVSg_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgAK0B0VSgSo23NSURLSessionTaskMetricsCSgSds6ResultOyxq_Gtcfc) `
    
    Creates a `DataResponse` instance with the specified parameters derived from the response serialization.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | The `URLRequest` sent to the server. |
    | `_response_` | The `HTTPURLResponse` from the server. |
    | `_data_` | The `Data` returned by the server. |
    | `_metrics_` | The `URLSessionTaskMetrics` of the `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) ` or `[UploadRequest](../Classes/UploadRequest.html) `. |
    | `_serializationDuration_` | The duration taken by serialization. |
    | `_result_` | The `Result` of response serialization. |
    
*   `[description](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV11descriptionSSvp) `
    
    The textual representation used when written to an output stream, which includes whether the result was a success or failure.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[debugDescription](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV16debugDescriptionSSvp) `
    
    The debug textual representation used when written to an output stream, which includes (if available) a summary of the `URLRequest`, the request’s headers and body (if decodable as a `String` below 100KB); the `HTTPURLResponse`‘s status code, headers, and body; the duration of the network and serialization actions; and the `Result` of serialization.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[map(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV3mapyACyqd__q_Gqd__xXEs8SendableRd__lF) `
    
    Evaluates the specified closure when the result of this `DataResponse` is a success, passing the unwrapped result value as a parameter.
    
    Use the `map` method with a closure that does not throw. For example:
    
        let possibleData: DataResponse<Data> = ...
        let possibleInt = possibleData.map { $0.count }
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_transform_` | A closure that takes the success value of the instance’s result. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A `DataResponse` whose result wraps the value returned by the given closure. If this instance’s result is a failure, returns a response wrapping the same failure.
    
*   `[tryMap(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV6tryMapyACyqd__s5Error_pGqd__xKXEs8SendableRd__lF) `
    
    Evaluates the given closure when the result of this `DataResponse` is a success, passing the unwrapped result value as a parameter.
    
    Use the `tryMap` method with a closure that may throw an error. For example:
    
        let possibleData: DataResponse<Data> = ...
        let possibleObject = possibleData.tryMap {
            try JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: $0)
        }
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_transform_` | A closure that takes the success value of the instance’s result. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A success or failure `DataResponse` depending on the result of the given closure. If this instance’s result is a failure, returns the same failure.
    
*   `[mapError(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV8mapErroryACyxqd__Gqd__q_XEs0E0Rd__lF) `
    
    Evaluates the specified closure when the `DataResponse` is a failure, passing the unwrapped error as a parameter.
    
    Use the `mapError` function with a closure that does not throw. For example:
    
        let possibleData: DataResponse<Data> = ...
        let withMyError = possibleData.mapError { MyError.error($0) }
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_transform_` | A closure that takes the error of the instance. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A `DataResponse` instance containing the result of the transform.
    
*   `[tryMapError(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire12DataResponseV11tryMapErroryACyxs0F0_pGqd__q_KXEsAERd__lF) `
    
    Evaluates the specified closure when the `DataResponse` is a failure, passing the unwrapped error as a parameter.
    
    Use the `tryMapError` function with a closure that may throw an error. For example:
    
        let possibleData: DataResponse<Data> = ...
        let possibleObject = possibleData.tryMapError {
            try someFailableFunction(taking: $0)
        }
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_transform_` | A throwing closure that takes the error of the instance. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A `DataResponse` instance containing the result of the transform.

---

# AlamofireExtension Structure Reference

AlamofireExtension
==================

Type that acts as a generic extension point for all `[AlamofireExtended](../Protocols/AlamofireExtended.html) ` types.

*   `[type](#/s:9Alamofire0A9ExtensionV4typexvp) `
    
    Stores the type or meta-type of any extended type.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire0A9ExtensionVyACyxGxcfc) `
    
    Create an instance from the provided value.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_type_` | Instance being extended. |
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60ExtendedType%60%3A%20%60URLSessionConfiguration%60)

### Available where `ExtendedType`: `URLSessionConfiguration`

*   `[default](#/s:9Alamofire0A9ExtensionVAASo25NSURLSessionConfigurationCRbzlE7defaultAEvpZ) `
    
    Alamofire’s default configuration. Same as `URLSessionConfiguration.default` but adds Alamofire default `Accept-Language`, `Accept-Encoding`, and `User-Agent` headers.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[ephemeral](#/s:9Alamofire0A9ExtensionVAASo25NSURLSessionConfigurationCRbzlE9ephemeralAEvpZ) `
    
    `.ephemeral` configuration with Alamofire’s default `Accept-Language`, `Accept-Encoding`, and `User-Agent` headers.
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60ExtendedType%60%3A%20%60Bundle%60)

### Available where `ExtendedType`: `Bundle`

*   `[certificates](#/s:9Alamofire0A9ExtensionVAASo8NSBundleCRbzlE12certificatesSaySo17SecCertificateRefaGvp) `
    
    Returns all valid `cer`, `crt`, and `der` certificates in the bundle.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[publicKeys](#/s:9Alamofire0A9ExtensionVAASo8NSBundleCRbzlE10publicKeysSaySo9SecKeyRefaGvp) `
    
    Returns all public keys for the valid certificates in the bundle.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[paths(forResourcesOfTypes:)](#/s:9Alamofire0A9ExtensionVAASo8NSBundleCRbzlE5paths19forResourcesOfTypesSaySSGAH_tF) `
    
    Returns all pathnames for the resources identified by the provided file extensions.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_types_` | The filename extensions locate. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    All pathnames for the given filename extensions.
    

[](#/Available%20where%20%60ExtendedType%60%20%3D%3D%20%60SecTrust%60)

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |

    #### Declaration

# DataResponsePublisher Structure Reference

DataResponsePublisher
=====================

A Combine `Publisher` that publishes the `DataResponse<Value, AFError>` of the provided `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) `.

*   `[Output](#/s:7Combine9PublisherP6OutputQa) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[Failure](#/s:7Combine9PublisherP7FailureQa) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(_:queue:serializer:)](#/s:9Alamofire21DataResponsePublisherV_5queue10serializerACyxGAA0B7RequestC_So012OS_dispatch_E0Cqd__tc16SerializedObjectQyd__RszAA0C10SerializerRd__lufc) `
    
    Creates an instance which will serialize responses using the provided `[ResponseSerializer](../Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) ` for which to publish the response. |
    | `_queue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which the `[DataResponse](../Structs/DataResponse.html) ` value will be published. `.main` by default. |
    | `_serializer_` | `[ResponseSerializer](../Protocols/ResponseSerializer.html) ` used to produce the published `[DataResponse](../Structs/DataResponse.html) `. |
    
*   `[init(_:queue:serializer:)](#/s:9Alamofire21DataResponsePublisherV_5queue10serializerACyxGAA0B7RequestC_So012OS_dispatch_E0Cqd__tc16SerializedObjectQyd__RszAA0bC18SerializerProtocolRd__lufc) `

    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | `[DataRequest](../Classes/DataRequest.html) ` for which to publish the response. |
    | `_queue_` | `DispatchQueue` on which the `[DataResponse](../Structs/DataResponse.html) ` value will be published. `.main` by default. |
    | `_serializer_` | `[DataResponseSerializerProtocol](../Protocols/DataResponseSerializerProtocol.html) ` used to produce the published `[DataResponse](../Structs/DataResponse.html) `. |
    
*   `[result()](#/s:9Alamofire21DataResponsePublisherV6result7Combine03AnyD0Vys6ResultOyxAA7AFErrorOGs5NeverOGyF) `
    
    Publishes only the `Result` of the `[DataResponse](../Structs/DataResponse.html) ` value.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Return Value

*   `[value()](#/s:9Alamofire21DataResponsePublisherV5value7Combine03AnyD0VyxAA7AFErrorOGyF) `
    
    Publishes the `Result` of the `[DataResponse](../Structs/DataResponse.html) ` as a single `Value` or fail with the `[AFError](../Enums/AFError.html) ` instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The `AnyPublisher<Value, AFError>` publishing the stream.
    
*   `[receive(subscriber:)](#/s:7Combine9PublisherP7receive10subscriberyqd___tAA10SubscriberRd__7FailureQyd__AGRtz5InputQyd__6OutputRtzlF) `
    
    #### Declaration

DataStreamPublisher

Undocumented

# DeflateRequestCompressor Structure Reference

DeflateRequestCompressor
========================

*   `[DuplicateHeaderBehavior](#/s:9Alamofire24DeflateRequestCompressorV23DuplicateHeaderBehaviorO) `

    #### Declaration
    
*   `[duplicateHeaderBehavior](#/s:9Alamofire24DeflateRequestCompressorV23duplicateHeaderBehaviorAC09DuplicatefG0Ovp) `
    
    Behavior to use when the outgoing `URLRequest` already has a `Content-Encoding` header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[shouldCompressBodyData](#/s:9Alamofire24DeflateRequestCompressorV22shouldCompressBodyDataySb10Foundation0H0VYbcvp) `

    #### Declaration

    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |

    | `_shouldCompressBodyData_` | Closure which determines whether the outgoing body data should be compressed. `true` by default. |

# DuplicateHeaderBehavior Enumeration Reference

DuplicateHeaderBehavior
=======================

Type that determines the action taken when the `URLRequest` already has a `Content-Encoding` header.

*   `[error](#/s:9Alamofire24DeflateRequestCompressorV23DuplicateHeaderBehaviorO5erroryA2EmF) `
    
    Throws a `[DuplicateHeaderError](../../Structs/DeflateRequestCompressor.html#/s:9Alamofire24DeflateRequestCompressorV20DuplicateHeaderErrorV) `. The default.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[replace](#/s:9Alamofire24DeflateRequestCompressorV23DuplicateHeaderBehaviorO7replaceyA2EmF) `
    
    Replaces the existing header value with `deflate`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[skip](#/s:9Alamofire24DeflateRequestCompressorV23DuplicateHeaderBehaviorO4skipyA2EmF) `
    
    Silently skips compression when the header exists.
    
    #### Declaration

# DownloadResponse Structure Reference

DownloadResponse
================

Used to store all data associated with a serialized response of a download request.

*   `[request](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV7request10Foundation10URLRequestVSgvp) `
    
    The URL request sent to the server.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[response](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV8responseSo17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgvp) `
    
    The server’s response to the URL request.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[fileURL](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV7fileURL10Foundation0E0VSgvp) `
    
    The final destination URL of the data returned from the server after it is moved.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[resumeData](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV10resumeData10Foundation0E0VSgvp) `
    
    The resume data generated if the request was cancelled.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[metrics](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV7metricsSo23NSURLSessionTaskMetricsCSgvp) `
    
    The final metrics of the response.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[serializationDuration](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV21serializationDurationSdvp) `
    
    The time taken to serialize the response.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[result](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV6results6ResultOyxq_Gvp) `
    
    The result of response serialization.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[value](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV5valuexSgvp) `
    
    Returns the associated value of the result if it is a success, `nil` otherwise.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[error](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV5errorq_Sgvp) `
    
    Returns the associated error value if the result if it is a failure, `nil` otherwise.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(request:response:fileURL:resumeData:metrics:serializationDuration:result:)](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV7request8response7fileURL10resumeData7metrics21serializationDuration6resultACyxq_G10Foundation10URLRequestVSg_So17NSHTTPURLResponseCSgAL0G0VSgAL0I0VSgSo23NSURLSessionTaskMetricsCSgSds6ResultOyxq_Gtcfc) `
    
    Creates a `DownloadResponse` instance with the specified parameters derived from response serialization.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_request_` | The `URLRequest` sent to the server. |
    | `_response_` | The `HTTPURLResponse` from the server. |
    | `_fileURL_` | The final destination URL of the data returned from the server after it is moved. |
    | `_resumeData_` | The resume `Data` generated if the request was cancelled. |
    | `_metrics_` | The `URLSessionTaskMetrics` of the `[DownloadRequest](../Classes/DownloadRequest.html) `. |
    | `_serializationDuration_` | The duration taken by serialization. |
    | `_result_` | The `Result` of response serialization. |
    
*   `[description](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV11descriptionSSvp) `
    
    The textual representation used when written to an output stream, which includes whether the result was a success or failure.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[debugDescription](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV16debugDescriptionSSvp) `
    
    The debug textual representation used when written to an output stream, which includes the URL request, the URL response, the temporary and destination URLs, the resume data, the durations of the network and serialization actions, and the response serialization result.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[map(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV3mapyACyqd__q_Gqd__xXEs8SendableRd__lF) `
    
    Evaluates the given closure when the result of this `DownloadResponse` is a success, passing the unwrapped result value as a parameter.
    
    Use the `map` method with a closure that does not throw. For example:
    
        let possibleData: DownloadResponse<Data> = ...
        let possibleInt = possibleData.map { $0.count }
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_transform_` | A closure that takes the success value of the instance’s result. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A `DownloadResponse` whose result wraps the value returned by the given closure. If this instance’s result is a failure, returns a response wrapping the same failure.
    
*   `[tryMap(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV6tryMapyACyqd__s5Error_pGqd__xKXEs8SendableRd__lF) `
    
    Evaluates the given closure when the result of this `DownloadResponse` is a success, passing the unwrapped result value as a parameter.
    
    Use the `tryMap` method with a closure that may throw an error. For example:
    
        let possibleData: DownloadResponse<Data> = ...
        let possibleObject = possibleData.tryMap {
            try JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: $0)
        }
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_transform_` | A closure that takes the success value of the instance’s result. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A success or failure `DownloadResponse` depending on the result of the given closure. If this instance’s result is a failure, returns the same failure.
    
*   `[mapError(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV8mapErroryACyxqd__Gqd__q_XEs0E0Rd__lF) `
    
    Evaluates the specified closure when the `DownloadResponse` is a failure, passing the unwrapped error as a parameter.
    
    Use the `mapError` function with a closure that does not throw. For example:
    
        let possibleData: DownloadResponse<Data> = ...
        let withMyError = possibleData.mapError { MyError.error($0) }
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_transform_` | A closure that takes the error of the instance. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A `DownloadResponse` instance containing the result of the transform.
    
*   `[tryMapError(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire16DownloadResponseV11tryMapErroryACyxs0F0_pGqd__q_KXEsAERd__lF) `
    
    Evaluates the specified closure when the `DownloadResponse` is a failure, passing the unwrapped error as a parameter.
    
    Use the `tryMapError` function with a closure that may throw an error. For example:
    
        let possibleData: DownloadResponse<Data> = ...
        let possibleObject = possibleData.tryMapError {
            try someFailableFunction(taking: $0)
        }
        
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_transform_` | A throwing closure that takes the error of the instance. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A `DownloadResponse` instance containing the result of the transform.

---

*   `[receive(subscriber:)](#/s:7Combine9PublisherP7receive10subscriberyqd___tAA10SubscriberRd__7FailureQyd__AGRtz5InputQyd__6OutputRtzlF) `
    
    #### Declaration

### Available where `Value` == `URL`?

# HTTPHeaders Structure Reference

HTTPHeaders
===========

An order-preserving and case-insensitive representation of HTTP headers.

*   `[init()](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersVACycfc) `
    
    Creates an empty instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersVyACSayAA10HTTPHeaderVGcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance from an array of `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) `s. Duplicate case-insensitive names are collapsed into the last name and value encountered.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersVyACSDyS2SGcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance from a `[String: String]`. Duplicate case-insensitive names are collapsed into the last name and value encountered.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[add(name:value:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV3add4name5valueySS_SStF) `
    
    Case-insensitively updates or appends an `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` into the instance using the provided `name` and `value`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_name_` | The `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` name. |
    | `_value_` | The `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` value. |
    
*   `[add(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV3addyyAA10HTTPHeaderVF) `
    
    Case-insensitively updates or appends the provided `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` into the instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_header_` | The `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` to update or append. |
    
*   `[update(name:value:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV6update4name5valueySS_SStF) `
    
    Case-insensitively updates or appends an `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` into the instance using the provided `name` and `value`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_name_` | The `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` name. |
    | `_value_` | The `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` value. |
    
*   `[update(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV6updateyyAA10HTTPHeaderVF) `
    
    Case-insensitively updates or appends the provided `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` into the instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_header_` | The `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` to update or append. |
    
*   `[remove(name:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV6remove4nameySS_tF) `
    
    Case-insensitively removes an `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) `, if it exists, from the instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_name_` | The name of the `[HTTPHeader](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html) ` to remove. |
    
*   `[sort()](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV4sortyyF) `
    
    Sort the current instance by header name, case insensitively.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[sorted()](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV6sortedACyF) `
    
    Returns an instance sorted by header name.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Return Value
    
    A copy of the current instance sorted by name.
    
*   `[value(for:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV5value3forSSSgSS_tF) `
    
    Case-insensitively find a header’s value by name.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_name_` | The name of the header to search for, case-insensitively. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The value of header, if it exists.
    
*   `[subscript(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersVySSSgSScip) `
    
    Case-insensitively access the header with the given name.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_name_` | The name of the header. |
    
*   `[dictionary](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV10dictionarySDyS2SGvp) `
    
    The dictionary representation of all headers.
    
    This representation does not preserve the current order of the instance.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(dictionaryLiteral:)](#/s:s30ExpressibleByDictionaryLiteralP010dictionaryD0x3KeyQz_5ValueQztd_tcfc) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(arrayLiteral:)](#/s:s25ExpressibleByArrayLiteralP05arrayD0x0cD7ElementQzd_tcfc) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[makeIterator()](#/s:ST12makeIterator0B0QzyF) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[startIndex](#/s:Sl10startIndex0B0Qzvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[endIndex](#/s:Sl8endIndex0B0Qzvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[subscript(_:)](#/s:Sly7ElementQz5IndexQzcip) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[index(after:)](#/s:Sl5index5after5IndexQzAD_tF) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[description](#/s:s23CustomStringConvertibleP11descriptionSSvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Defaults)

### Defaults

*   `[default](#/s:9Alamofire11HTTPHeadersV7defaultACvpZ) `
    
    The default set of `HTTPHeaders` used by Alamofire. Includes `Accept-Encoding`, `Accept-Language`, and `User-Agent`.
    
    #### Declaration
