# HTTPMethod Structure Reference

HTTPMethod
==========

Type representing HTTP methods. Raw `String` value is stored and compared case-sensitively, so `HTTPMethod.get != HTTPMethod(rawValue: "get")`.

See [https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-4.3](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-4.3)

*   `[connect](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV7connectACvpZ) `
    
    `CONNECT` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[delete](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV6deleteACvpZ) `
    
    `DELETE` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[get](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV3getACvpZ) `
    
    `GET` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[head](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV4headACvpZ) `
    
    `HEAD` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[options](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV7optionsACvpZ) `
    
    `OPTIONS` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[patch](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV5patchACvpZ) `
    
    `PATCH` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[post](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV4postACvpZ) `
    
    `POST` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[put](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV3putACvpZ) `
    
    `PUT` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[query](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV5queryACvpZ) `
    
    `QUERY` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[trace](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPMethodV5traceACvpZ) `
    
    `TRACE` method.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[rawValue](#/s:SY8rawValue03RawB0Qzvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(rawValue:)](#/s:SY8rawValuexSg03RawB0Qz_tcfc) `
    
    #### Declaration

---

# HTTPHeader Structure Reference

HTTPHeader
==========

A representation of a single HTTP header’s name / value pair.

*   `[name](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV4nameSSvp) `
    
    Name of the header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[value](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV5valueSSvp) `
    
    Value of the header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(name:value:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV4name5valueACSS_SStcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance from the given `[name](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV4nameSSvp) ` and `[value](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV5valueSSvp) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_name_` | The name of the header. |
    | `_value_` | The value of the header. |
    

[](#/HTTPHeader)

### HTTPHeader

*   `[description](#/s:s23CustomStringConvertibleP11descriptionSSvp) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[accept(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV6acceptyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns an `Accept` header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Accept` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[acceptCharset(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV13acceptCharsetyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns an `Accept-Charset` header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Accept-Charset` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[acceptLanguage(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV14acceptLanguageyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns an `Accept-Language` header.
    
    Alamofire offers a default Accept-Language header that accumulates and encodes the system’s preferred languages. Use `[HTTPHeader.defaultAcceptLanguage](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV21defaultAcceptLanguageACvpZ) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Accept-Language` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[acceptEncoding(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV14acceptEncodingyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns an `Accept-Encoding` header.
    
    Alamofire offers a default accept encoding value that provides the most common values. Use `[HTTPHeader.defaultAcceptEncoding](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV21defaultAcceptEncodingACvpZ) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Accept-Encoding` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header
    
*   `[authorization(username:password:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV13authorization8username8passwordACSS_SStFZ) `
    
    Returns a `Basic` `Authorization` header using the `username` and `password` provided.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_username_` | The username of the header. |
    | `_password_` | The password of the header. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[authorization(bearerToken:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV13authorization11bearerTokenACSS_tFZ) `
    
    Returns a `Bearer` `Authorization` header using the `bearerToken` provided.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_bearerToken_` | The bearer token. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[authorization(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV13authorizationyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns an `Authorization` header.
    
    Alamofire provides built-in methods to produce `Authorization` headers. For a Basic `Authorization` header use `[HTTPHeader.authorization(username:password:)](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV13authorization8username8passwordACSS_SStFZ) `. For a Bearer `Authorization` header, use `[HTTPHeader.authorization(bearerToken:)](../Structs/HTTPHeader.html#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV13authorization11bearerTokenACSS_tFZ) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Authorization` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[contentDisposition(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV18contentDispositionyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns a `Content-Disposition` header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Content-Disposition` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[contentEncoding(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV15contentEncodingyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns a `Content-Encoding` header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Content-Encoding`. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[contentType(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV11contentTypeyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns a `Content-Type` header.
    
    All Alamofire `[ParameterEncoding](../Protocols/ParameterEncoding.html) `s and `[ParameterEncoder](../Protocols/ParameterEncoder.html) `s set the `Content-Type` of the request, so it may not be necessary to manually set this value.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Content-Type` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[userAgent(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV9userAgentyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns a `User-Agent` header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `User-Agent` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    
*   `[websocketProtocol(_:)](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV17websocketProtocolyACSSFZ) `
    
    Returns a `Sec-WebSocket-Protocol` header.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_value_` | The `Sec-WebSocket-Protocol` value. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The header.
    

[](#/Defaults)

### Defaults

*   `[defaultAcceptEncoding](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV21defaultAcceptEncodingACvpZ) `
    
    Returns Alamofire’s default `Accept-Encoding` header, appropriate for the encodings supported by particular OS versions.
    
    See the [Accept-Encoding HTTP header documentation](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-4.2.3)
     .
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultAcceptLanguage](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV21defaultAcceptLanguageACvpZ) `
    
    Returns Alamofire’s default `Accept-Language` header, generated by querying `Locale` for the user’s `preferredLanguages`.
    
    See the [Accept-Language HTTP header documentation](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-5.3.5)
    .
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[defaultUserAgent](#/s:9Alamofire10HTTPHeaderV16defaultUserAgentACvpZ) `
    
    Returns Alamofire’s default `User-Agent` header.
    
    See the [User-Agent header documentation](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-5.5.3)
    .
    
    Example: `iOS Example/1.0 (org.alamofire.iOS-Example; build:1; iOS 13.0.0) Alamofire/5.0.0`
    
    #### Declaration

---

# JSONEncoding Structure Reference

JSONEncoding
============

Uses `JSONSerialization` to create a JSON representation of the parameters object, which is set as the body of the request. The `Content-Type` HTTP header field of an encoded request is set to `application/json`.

*   `[Error](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV5ErrorO) `
    
    Error produced by `[JSONEncoding](../Structs/JSONEncoding.html) `.
    
    [See more](../Structs/JSONEncoding/Error.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Properties)

### Properties

*   `[default](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV7defaultACvpZ) `
    
    Returns a `JSONEncoding` instance with default writing options.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[prettyPrinted](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV13prettyPrintedACvpZ) `
    
    Returns a `JSONEncoding` instance with `.prettyPrinted` writing options.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[options](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV7optionsSo20NSJSONWritingOptionsVvp) `
    
    The options for writing the parameters as JSON data.
    
    #### Declaration
    

[](#/Initialization)

### Initialization

*   `[init(options:)](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV7optionsACSo20NSJSONWritingOptionsV_tcfc) `
    
    Creates an instance using the specified `WritingOptions`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_options_` | `JSONSerialization.WritingOptions` to use. |
    

[](#/Encoding)

### Encoding

*   `[encode(_:with:)](#/s:9Alamofire17ParameterEncodingP6encode_4with10Foundation10URLRequestVAA0G11Convertible_p_SDySSs8Sendable_pGSgtKF) `
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[encode(_:withJSONObject:)](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV6encode_14withJSONObject10Foundation10URLRequestVAA0G11Convertible_p_ypSgtKF) `
    
    Encodes any JSON compatible object into a `URLRequest`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_urlRequest_` | `[URLRequestConvertible](../Protocols/URLRequestConvertible.html) ` value into which the object will be encoded. |
    | `_jsonObject_` | `Any` value (must be JSON compatible) to be encoded into the `URLRequest`. `nil` by default. |
    
    #### Return Value
    
    The encoded `URLRequest`.

---

# Error Enumeration Reference

Error
=====

Error produced by `[JSONEncoding](../../Structs/JSONEncoding.html) `.

*   `[invalidJSONObject](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV5ErrorO17invalidJSONObjectyA2EmF) `
    
    `[JSONEncoding](../../Structs/JSONEncoding.html) ` attempted to encode an invalid JSON object. Usually this means the value included types not representable in Objective-C. See `JSONSerialization.isValidJSONObject` for details.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[localizedDescription](#/s:9Alamofire12JSONEncodingV5ErrorO20localizedDescriptionSSvp) `
    
    Undocumented
    
    #### Declaration

# ResponseCacher Structure Reference

ResponseCacher
==============

`ResponseCacher` is a convenience `[CachedResponseHandler](../Protocols/CachedResponseHandler.html) ` making it easy to cache, not cache, or modify a cached response.

*   `[Behavior](#/s:9Alamofire14ResponseCacherV8BehaviorO) `
    
    Defines the behavior of the `[ResponseCacher](../Structs/ResponseCacher.html) ` type.
    
    [See more](../Structs/ResponseCacher/Behavior.html)
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[cache](#/s:9Alamofire14ResponseCacherV5cacheACvpZ) `
    
    Returns a `ResponseCacher` with a `.cache` `[Behavior](../Structs/ResponseCacher/Behavior.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[doNotCache](#/s:9Alamofire14ResponseCacherV10doNotCacheACvpZ) `
    
    Returns a `ResponseCacher` with a `.doNotCache` `[Behavior](../Structs/ResponseCacher/Behavior.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[behavior](#/s:9Alamofire14ResponseCacherV8behaviorAC8BehaviorOvp) `
    
    The `[Behavior](../Structs/ResponseCacher/Behavior.html) ` of the `ResponseCacher`.
    
    #### Declaration
    
*   `[init(behavior:)](#/s:9Alamofire14ResponseCacherV8behaviorA2C8BehaviorO_tcfc) `
    
    Creates a `ResponseCacher` instance from the `[Behavior](../Structs/ResponseCacher/Behavior.html) `.
    
    #### Declaration
    
    #### Parameters
    
    |     |     |
    | --- | --- |
    | `_behavior_` | The `[Behavior](../Structs/ResponseCacher/Behavior.html) `. |
    
*   `[dataTask(_:willCacheResponse:completion:)](#/s:9Alamofire21CachedResponseHandlerP8dataTask_09willCacheC010completionySo016NSURLSessionDataF0C_So19NSCachedURLResponseCyAJSgctF) `
    
    #### Declaration
